[\[1b.1\]{D3720}]@##//rgya gar skad du/_ma hA yA na me la pa na pra dI paM/_bod skad du/_theg pa chen po bsdus pa'i sgron ma/_sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad la phyag 'tshal
[\[1b.2\]]lo/_/nyes pa'i dri ma ma lus spangs shing chos nyid zab mo rgya mtsho lta bu gzigs/_/thugs rjes 'khor ba ji srid bar du bzhugs shing gzhan gyi don mdzad pa'i/_/thub pa'i dbang po sras dang
[\[1b.3\]]bcas pa rnams la phyag 'tshal lo/_/mdo rgyud kun las btus pa'i theg chen bsdus pa'i sgron ma 'di/_/ma rig dbang du song ba'i sems can rnams kyi don du bdag gis rab gsal bya/_/de la
[\[1b.4\]]rigs kyi bu'am rigs kyi bu mo rigs dang skal ba dang ldan pa des sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la ji ltar 'jug par bya zhe na/_des ni sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la rim gyis 'jug pa la bslab par bya'i
[\[1b.5\]]cig car ni ma yin te/_de ltar yang bcom ldan 'das kyis lang kar gshegs pa'i mdo las gsungs te/_bcom ldan 'das la byang chub sems dpa' blo gros chen pos zhus pa/_bcom
[\[2a\]]
[\[2a.1\]]ldan 'das rang gi sems rim gyis sam cig car gyis dag par 'gyur lags/_bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_blo gros chen po rang gi sems ni rim gyis 'jug pas rnam par dag ste cig car
[\[2a.2\]]ni ma yin no/_/blo gros chen po 'di lta ste shing a mra'i 'bras bu ni rim gyis smin par 'gyur gyi cig car ni ma yin no/_/blo gros chen po de bzhin du sems can rnams kyi sems kyang rim gyis rnam par dag ste cig car ni ma
[\[2a.3\]]yin no/_/blo gros chen po 'di lta ste rdza mkhan gyis snod rnams ni rim gyis byed kyi cig car ni ma yin no/_/blo gros chen po de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa yang sems can rnams kyi sems rim gyis rnam par spyod ste cig
[\[2a.4\]]car ni ma yin no/_/blo gros chen po 'di lta ste sa chen po las rtsa ba dang shing gel pa dang sman dang nags tshal rnams rim gyis 'jug par skye'i cig car ni ma yin no/_/de bzhin du blo gros chen po de bzhin gshegs pa yang
[\[2a.5\]]sems can rnams kyi sems rim gyis sbyong ste cig car ni ma yin no/_/blo gros chen po 'di lta ste bzhad gad dang /_rol mo dang /_glu dang pi wang dang /_sil snyan dang /_rol mo la mkhas pa ni rim gyis 'byung gi cig car ni ma
[\[2b\]]
[\[2b.1\]]yin no/_/de bzhin du blo gros chen po de bzhin gshegs pa yang sems can rnams kyi sems rim gyis rnam par sbyong ste cig car ni ma yin no/_/rim pa 'di gnyis ni sa'i snying po'i mdo las gsungs te/_gang la mtho ris theg pa yod min/_/de la nyan thos theg pa med de/_
[\[2b.2\]]gang la nyan thos theg pa yod min/_/de la rang rgyal theg pa med de/_/gang la rang rgyal theg pa yod min/_/de la theg pa chen po med de/_/zhes gsungs so/_/sems can dang po'i las can rnams/_/dam pa'i chos la 'jug pa la/_/thabs 'di rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas
[\[2b.3\]]kyis/_/skas kyi rim pa lta bur gsungs/_/des na sangs rgyas kyi bstan pa la rim gyis bslab par bya'o/_/de'i phyir rigs kyi bu'am rigs kyi bu mo dal 'byor gyi rten thob pa rigs dang skal ba dang ldan pa des dang po dkon mchog gsum la skyabs su phyin la/_dad pa dang ngo tsha
[\[2b.4\]]shes pa dang khrel yod pa dang ldan pa des srog gcod pa dang /_ma byin par len pa dang /_mi tshangs par spyod pa dang /_brdzun dang /_phra ma dang /_ngag 'khyal pa dang /_tshig rtsub mo dang /_brnab sems dang /_gnod sems dang /_log lta dang /_chang spang ba dang /_dran pa dang /_shes
[\[2b.5\]]bzhin dang /_bag yod pa la gnas par bya'o/_/rin po che'i phreng ba las/_gsod pa yis ni tshe thung 'gyur/_/rnam par 'tshe ba gnod pa mang /_/rku ba yis ni longs spyod phongs/_/byi po byed pa dgra dang bcas/_/brdzun du smra bas skur pa ste/_/phra ma yis ni bshes dang 'bye/_/tshig
[\[2b.6\]]rtsub kyis ni mi snyan thos/_/ma 'brel pa yis tshig mi btsun/_/brnab sems yid la re ba 'joms/_/gnod sems 'jigs pa sbyin par bshad/_/log par lta bas lta ngan nyid/_/chang 'thung ba yis blo 'khrul te/_/ma byin pas ni dbul ba nyid/_/log pas 'tsho
[\[2b.7\]]bas slu ba ste/_/khengs pa yis ni rigs ngan nyid/_/phrag dog gis ni gzi chung nyid/_/khro bas kha dog ngan pa nyid/_/mkhas la mi 'dri blun pa nyid/_/mi nyid la ni 'bras bu 'di/_/kun gyi dang por ngan 'gro'o/_/mi dge zhes bya de dag gi_/rnam smin grags pa gang yin pa/_/
[\[3a\]]
[\[3a.1\]]dge ba dag ni thams cad la/_/'bras bu de ni bzlog ste 'byung /_/chags dang zhe sdang gti mug dang /_/des bskyed las ni mi dge ba/_/ma chags zhe sdang gti mug med/_/des bskyed las ni dge ba yin/_/mi dge ba las sdug bsngal kun/_/de bzhin
[\[3a.2\]]ngan 'gro thams cad do/_/dge las bde 'gro thams cad dang /_/skye ba kun du bde ba dag_/'byung ba 'di la the tshom med/_/yid dang lus dang ngag gis ni/_/mi dge kun las ldog bya zhing /_/dge la rtag tu 'jug par bya/_/chos 'di rnam pa gnyis su bshad/_/chos 'dis
[\[3a.3\]]dmyal ba yi dgas dang /_/dud 'gro dag las rnam grol zhing /_/lha dang mi yi nang dag tu/_/bde dpal rgyal srid rgyas pa thob/_/bsam gtan tshad med gzugs med ni/_/tshangs sogs bde ba myong bar byed/_/de ltar mtho ris chos 'di dang /_/de yi 'bras bu mdor
[\[3a.4\]]bsdus pa'o/_/zhes gsungs so/_/des ni mi dge ba bcu las log cing 'khor ba la yid spro ba bzlog ste yid ches pa'i dad pa dang dad pa'i dad pa dang /_'dod pa'i dad pa brtan po bskyed la srog gis bsdus pa'i sems can thams cad la byams pa dang snying rje sngon du 'gro bas
[\[3a.5\]]sems can la blta ba'i sems kyis dkon mchog gsum la snying po byang chub la thug gi bar du skyabs su 'gro ba dang /_dge ba'i bshes gnyen mkhas pa dang /_btsun pa dang /_snying rje dang ldan pa dang /_chos dang zang zing la ser sna dang phrag dog med cing bya ba la yid gzhungs pa
[\[3a.6\]]dang /_skyo ba med cing rigs dang spobs pa dang kha dog dang ldan pa la byang chub mchog tu sems bskyed par bya'o/_/de nas dad pa dang /_ngo tsha shes pa dang /_khrel yod pa dang /_dran pa dang /_shes bzhin dang /_bag yod pa la gnas te/_byang chub kyi sems dang /_sdom pa
[\[3a.7\]]dang 'gal ba'i las brtags te spang bar bya'o/_/srog gis bsdus pa'i sems can la byams pa dang /_snying rje sngon du 'gro bas srog gcod pa dang /_ma byin par len pa dang /_'dod pa la phyin ci log pa dang /_brdzun dang /_phra ma dang /_tshig rtsub dang /_ngag 'khyal pa dang /_brnab
[\[3b\]]
[\[3b.1\]]sems dang /_gnod sems dang /_log lta dang /_sha dang nya dang chang dang sgog pa dang la phug dang /_rgya skyegs kyi las dang /_til gyi las dang /_zhing las la sogs pa ni rtag tu spang bar bya'o/_/dge slong dang byang chub tu sems bskyed pa dang /_dam tshig dang ldan pa la gus par bya
[\[3b.2\]]zhing brnyas par mi bya'o/_/sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang ldan zhing rang la rnam par 'tshe ba la bzod par bya'o/_/byang chub kyi sems rgyun du bsgom zhing smon lam rgya chen po gdab par bya'o/_/bla ma dang /_dkon mchog dang /_phan 'dogs pa dang /_sdug bsngal ba dang /_nad pa dang /_nad
[\[3b.3\]]g.yog pa dang /_phra ma dang /_glo bur gyi mgron po dang /_bram ze la zas dang /_gos dang /_btung ba dang /_sman dang /_rin po che dang /_mar me dang /_dri dang /_spos dang /_yo byad kyi dngos po sbyin zhing /_lus dang bsod nams kyi dngos po thams cad gtong ba dang /_chos dang mi
[\[3b.4\]]'jigs pa sbyin pa dang /_gzhan gyis dgos pa'i grogs dang nad g.yog la sogs pa bya'o/_/rin po che'i phreng ba las/_gom pa bdun pa'i dus su yang /_/bdog pa kun gtong sems 'chang ba/_/byang chub sems dpa' rnams la ni/_/bsod nams mkha' 'dra dpag
[\[3b.5\]]med skye/_/gsung /_rgyal ba'i yum las kyang /_rab 'byor 'di ji snyam du sems shar phyogs kyi nam mkha' tshad gzung bar sla'am/_rab 'byor gyis gsol pa/_bcom ldan 'das de ni ma lags so/_/rab 'byor de bzhin du byang chub sems dpa' gang mi gnas par sbyin pa
[\[3b.6\]]yongs su gtong ba de'i bsod nams kyi phung po yang tshad gzung bar sla ba ma yin no/_/yang de nyid las/_rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na/_mig dang ldan pa'i mi zhig mun par zhugs na ci yang mi mthong ba de bzhin du gang dngos por ltung bas sbyin pa yongs su gtong ba'i byang chub sems
[\[3b.7\]]dpar blta'o/_/rab 'byor 'di lta ste dper na nam langs te nyi ma shar nas mig dang ldan pa'i mis gzugs rnam pa sna tshogs dag mthong ba de bzhin du gang dngos por ma lhung bas sbyin pa yongs su gtong ba'i byang chub sems dpar blta'o zhes gsungs so/_/des na gang sbyin pa de
[\[4a\]]
[\[4a.1\]]'khor gsum yongs su dag par byin na nyid byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyis phyin ci ma log pa'i sbyin pa ste mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyur 'gyur ba'o/_/de yang gti mug med pa'i dge ba'i rtsa ba'o/_/de bzhin du thos pa dang /_bsam pa dang /_bsgom pa dang /_
[\[4a.2\]]dka' thub la gnas pa dang /_gzhan gyi grogs byed pa'i tshe lus dang sems kyi sdug bsngal byung ba dang du blang ba dang /_de bzhin du bdag gi pa la gnod pa mthong ba'i tshe gnyen po bsran thub par bya ba dang /_gnod pa byed pa dang /_gnod pa'i dngos po dang /_gnod bya rnams sgyu ma
[\[4a.3\]]lta bu dang stong par shes te bzod pa la gnas par bya'o/_/de ltar bzod pa la gnas pa'i gang zag ni 'di nyid la lus dang sems bde ba dang /_'khor mang ba dang /_lha la sogs pa srung ba dang /_tshe 'phos nas kyang sangs rgyas kyi zhing khams dag par skye ba dang /_rigs bzang ba
[\[4a.4\]]dang /_gzugs dang kha dog bzang ba dang /_nad med pa dang /_tshe ring ba dang /_'khor g.yog byams pa dang /_'byor pa phun sum tshogs par skye zhing mtho ris lha dang mi'i rgyal por 'gyur ba dang /_mthar thug mya ngan las 'das pa'i rgyur 'gyur ro/_/de ltar bzod pa dang ldan pa
[\[4a.5\]]des le lo dang snyom las dang zhum pa bsal te/_dge ba'i las la sems spro ba dang yid gzhungs par bya'o/_/le lo dang snyom las dang sems zhum pa la gnas na sbyin pa nas shes rab kyi bar du med do/_/bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi med do/_/sbyangs pa'i yon tan dang tshad med pa dang dran pa
[\[4a.6\]]nye bar gzhag pa dang /_yang dag par spong ba dang /_rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa dang /_dbang po lnga dang /_byang chub kyi yan lag bdun dang /_'phags pa'i lam yan lag brgyad thob pa med do/_/dkon mchog mchod pa dang /_gzhan gyi grogs bya ba dang /_dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa
[\[4a.7\]]med do/_/de'i phyir na dge ba'i las la dus rtag tu mgo dang gos la me 'bar ba gsod pa bzhin du bya'o/_/dkon mchog gsum dang bla ma dang grogs tshangs pa mtshungs par spyod pa dang /_bslab pa la gus pa bskyed par bya'o/_/sems can thams cad la pha dang ma dang /_mkhan
[\[4b\]]
[\[4b.1\]]po dang /_slob dpon dang /_ston pa'i 'du shes bskyed la ma gus pa dang /_brnyas pa dang /_zhe sdang dang /_khong khro dang /_nga rgyal dang /_khyad du gsod pa spang ba la nan tan bya ba dang /_de ltar dge ba la lus dang ngag dang sems las su rung na lus dang sems ldang ba yang ba dang /_
[\[4b.2\]]dge ba'i tshogs mang po dang ldan par 'gyur ro/_/de ltar dge ba la gnas pa'i gang zag la lha dang /_klu dang /_gnod sbyin dang /_dri za dang /_lha ma yin dang /_nam mkha'i lding dang /_lto 'phye chen po la sogs pa dga' zhing gus pa dang srung ba byed par 'gyur ro/_/de'i phyir 'dun pa
[\[4b.3\]]dang dad pa la gnas te dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten pa dang de la dam pa'i chos nyan pa dang tshul bzhin du bsam pa dang /_de'i don yid la bsgom pa dang /_bla ma dang dkon mchog la mchod pa dang /_bsdu ba'i dngos po bzhi dang /_'phags pa'i bden pa bzhi dang /_rjes su dran pa
[\[4b.4\]]drug dang /_'phags pa'i nor bdun yid la bya ba dang /_ngo tsha shes pa dang /_khrel yod pa la gnas te bslab pa la gus par bya ba dang /_gzhan gyi 'khrul pa la mi brtag pa dang /_rang gi 'khrul pa la brtag pa dang /_nga rgyal spangs te zhi zhing dul ba la gnas par bya ba dang /_dran
[\[4b.5\]]pa dang shes bzhin la gnas te/_lus dang ngag dang yid kyi las don yod par bya ba dang /_dben pa la gnas te zhi gnas dang lhag mthong bsgom pa dang /_'khor ba'i skyon dang mya ngan las 'das pa'i yon tan yid la bya ba dang /_chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bu dang /_chu zla lta bu dang /_mig
[\[4b.6\]]yor lta bu dang /_smig rgyu lta bu dang /_rmi lam lta bu dang /_brag ca lta bu dang /_dri za'i grong khyer lta bu dang /_mig 'phrul lta bu dang /_'ja' tshon lta bu dang /_glog lta bu dang /_chu'i chu bur lta bu dang /_me long gi gzugs brnyan lta bu ste/_sgyu ma'i dpe bcu gnyis lta bur yid la bya ba dang /_
[\[4b.7\]]rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal zhing skye ba med par yid la bya'o/_/de ltar dge ba la spro ba dang /_'dun pa dang /_dad par gyur pa'i gang zag des 'khor ba'i rtsa ba 'jig rten gyi chos brgyad la me dang /_mtshon dang /_dug dang /_zug rngu lta bu'i 'du shes bskyed pa ting nge 'dzin dang rjes su
[\[5a\]]
[\[5a.1\]]mthun pa'i gnas su zas kyi tshod rig pa dang /_srod dang tho rangs mi nyal bar rnal 'byor la brtson par bya'o/_/de yang yid du 'ong ba'i sems can nas phyogs bcu'i sems can thams cad la byams pa dang snying rje rgyun ma chad par rtag tu gus par bsgom par
[\[5a.2\]]bya'o/_/byams pa dang snying rjes rgyud brlan na zhe sdang dang khong khro zhi bar 'gyur ro/_/'phags pa klu sgrub kyi zhal nas kyang byams pa'i phan yon gsungs pa/_ro dang ldan pa'i kha zas dag_/nyin re dus gsum byin pa bas/_/byams pa yud tsam thang cig gi_/bsod nams gang
[\[5a.3\]]la char mi phod/_/lha mi byams par 'gyur ba dang /_/de dag kyang ni bsrung ba dang /_/yid bde ba dang bde mang dang /_/dug dang mtshon gyis gnod med dang /_/'bad pa med par longs spyod thob/_/tshangs pa'i 'jig rten skye 'gyur te/_/gal te grol bar ma gyur kyang /_/byams
[\[5a.4\]]chos yon tan brgyad thob bo/_/zhes gsungs so/_/gzhan yang byams pa dang snying rje'i phan yon ni zla ba sgron ma'i mdo dang chos yang dag par sdud pa'i mdo las shes par bya'o/_/gzhan yang rang dang gzhan gyi lus mi gtsang ba'i 'du shes rgyun ma chad par dus rtag tu yid la
[\[5a.5\]]bya'o/_/de ltar yang rin po che'i phreng ba las gsungs pa/_bud med chags pa phal cher ni/_/bud med gzugs gtsang sems las byung /_/bud med lus la don du ni/_/gtsang ba cung zad yod ma yin/_/kha ni kha chu rul ba dang /_/so rkyag mi gtsang snod yin no/_/sna ni
[\[5a.6\]]rnag snabs sna chu'i snod/_/mig ni mig rdul mchi ma'i snod/_/lto ba'i khong ni bshang gci dang /_/glo ba mchin pa'i snod yin no/_/rmongs pas bud med ma mthong ba/_/de yi lus la chags par byed/_/mi shes 'ga' zhig mi gtsang ba'i/_/bum pa brgyan la chags pa ltar/_/
[\[5a.7\]]'jig rten mi shes rmongs pa yis/_/bud med rnams la de bzhin no/_/lus rul shin tu dri nga ba/_/chags bral rgyu ni gang yin pa/_/de la'ang 'jig rten ches chags na/_/gang gis 'dod chags bral bar 'gyur/_/ji ltar bshang gci bcer ba la/_/khyi phag rab tu chags pa ltar/_/
[\[5b\]]
[\[5b.1\]]de bzhin bshang gci bcer ba la/_/'dod ldan rnams ni chags par 'gyur/_/lus kyi grong khyer mi gtsang ba/_/'byung ba'i bu ga dod pa gang /_/de ni skye bo blun po yis/_/dga' ba'i don du nye bar brtags/_/khyod rang nyid kyis bshang gci sogs/_/so sor mi gtsang
[\[5b.2\]]mthong nas ni/_/de 'dus lus la ji lta bur/_/yid du 'ong ba nyid du 'gyur/_/khrag dang khu ba 'dres pa yi/_/sa bon mi gtsang snying pos skyed/_/mi gtsang gzugs su shes bzhin du/_/'di la 'dod pa gang gis chags/_/mi gtsang phung po de'i rlan gyis/_/brlan pa
[\[5b.3\]]pags pas g.yogs pa gang /_/nyal ba de nyid bud med dang /_/lto ba sprad de nyal bar zad/_/gzugs bzang ba'am gzugs ngan nam/_/rgan nam yang na gzhon yang rung /_/bud med gzugs kun mi gtsang na/_/khyod chags khyad par ga la skye/_/gal te mi gtsang kha
[\[5b.4\]]dog bzang /_/shin tu gsal la dbyibs legs kyang /_/de la chags par mi 'os ltar/_/bud med gzugs la'ang de bzhin no/_/khong rul phyi rol pags pas g.yogs/_/ro myags 'di yi rang bzhin ni/_/shin tu mi bzad snang bzhin du/_/mi gtsang bar ni mthong
[\[5b.5\]]ma gyur/_/mi gtsang gang ba'i bum pa 'di/_/phyi rol bkra yang smad pa ltar/_/mi gtsang ba yi rang bzhin lus/_/mi gtsang gang ba cis mi smad/_/ji ltar bud med gzugs mi gtsang /_/khyod kyi rang lus de dang 'dra/_/de bas phyi dang nang nyid la/_/'dod chags bral ba
[\[5b.6\]]rigs min nam/_/rma dgu dag nas 'dzag pa can/_/bdag nyid mngon sum 'khru byed kyang /_/lus mi gtsang bar mi rtogs nas/_/khyod la bshad pas ci zhig phan/_/zhes gsungs so/_/gzhan yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa'i mdo dang dkon mchog sprin gyi mdo las
[\[5b.7\]]kyang shes par bya'o/_/sA lu ljang pa'i mdo las 'byung ba bzhin du phyi rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba dang /_nang rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba yang shes rab kyi mig gis blta bar bya'o/_/de ltar byams pa dang /_snying rje dang /_mi sdug pa dang /_rten cing 'brel par 'byung ba'i don
[\[6a\]]
[\[6a.1\]]yid la byed pa'o/_/'og nas lhag mthong bsgom pa'i dus su yang mdor na ting nge 'dzin thams cad kyi nyes pa drug yod de/_le lo dang /_dmigs pa brjed pa dang /_bying ba dang /_rgod pa dang /_mi rtsol ba dang rtsol ba'o/_/de rnams kyi gnyen
[\[6a.2\]]por spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad bsgom mo/_/'di lta ste dad pa dang /_'dun pa dang /_brtson 'grus dang /_shin tu sbyangs pa dang /_dran pa dang /_shes bzhin dang /_sems pa dang /_btang snyoms so/_/de la gong ma bzhi ni le lo'i gnyen po yin te/_'di ltar ting nge 'dzin gyi yon
[\[6a.3\]]tan dag la mngon par yid ches pa'i mtshan nyid dang ldan pa'i dad pas rnal 'byor pa rnams de la 'dod pa skye'o/_/de nas 'dod pas brtson 'grus rtsom mo/_/de brtson 'grus kyi stobs kyis lus dang sems las su rung ba nyid du byed do/_/de nas lus dang sems shin tu
[\[6a.4\]]sbyangs par gyur pas le lo ldog ste/_de bas na dad pa la sogs pa ni le lo spong ba'i gnyen po'o/_/dran pa ni dmigs pa brjed pa'i gnyen po'o/_/shes bzhin ni bying ba dang rgod pa'i gnyen po ste/_bying ba dang rgod pa yang dag par rtogs pa'i phyir ro/_/bying ba dang rgod pa rab
[\[6a.5\]]tu ma zhi ba'i dus na mi rtsol ba'i gnyen po ste/_de'i gnyen por sems pa bsgom mo/_/bying ba dang rgod pa rab tu zhi ste gang gi tshe sems rnal du 'jug pa de'i tshe rtsol ba nyes pa yin te/_de'i gnyen por de'i tshe btang snyoms bsgom mo/_/spong ba'i 'du byed brgyad po de dag dang
[\[6a.6\]]ldan na ting nge 'dzin shin tu skyon med par 'gyur ro/_/ting nge 'dzin la skyon med na rdzu 'phrul la sogs phan yon rnams sgrub par byed do/_/de ltar sems las su rung bar gyur pa des bden pa gnyis kyi don la 'jug par bya ste/_dbu ma rtsa ba las gsungs pa/_sangs rgyas
[\[6a.7\]]rnams kyis chos bstan pa/_/bden pa gnyis la yang dag brten/_/'jig rten kun rdzob bden pa dang /_/de bzhin don dam bden pa'o/_/gang gis bden pa gnyis po yi/_/rnam dbye rnam par mi shes pa/_/de dag sangs rgyas bstan pa yi/_/zab mo de dag rnam mi
[\[6b\]]
[\[6b.1\]]shes/_/zhes gsungs so/_/de la kun rdzob kyi bden pa ni rnam pa gnyis te/_yang dag pa'i kun rdzob dang /_log pa'i kun rdzob bo/_/de la yang dag pa'i kun rdzob ni ma brtags na nyams dga' ba don byed nus pa'i dngos po'o/_/log pa'i kun rdzob na snang bzhin du don
[\[6b.2\]]byed pas stong pa'i phyir ro/_/don dam pa'i bden pa ni rang bzhin gyis rnam par dag pa spros pa'i mtha' dang bral ba/_skye ba dang gnas pa dang 'gag pas stong pas brjod du med pa dbyibs dang bral ba'o/_/de ltar dri ma med par grags pa'i mdo las kyang /_gzugs kyi rang
[\[6b.3\]]bzhin ni stong pa ste bshig pas stong pa ni ma yin no/_/de bzhin du tshor ba nas rnam par shes pa'i bar du bshig pas stong pa ni ma yin te/_rang bzhin dang bral ba'i phyir ro zhes gsungs so/_/gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud las kyang /_rang sems gzod nas ma skyes pa/_/stong pa
[\[6b.4\]]nyid kyi rang bzhin no/_/zhes gsungs so/_/chos yang dag par sdud pa'i mdo las kyang gsungs te/_chos thams cad ni dmigs pa med pa ste de la rnam par shes pa mi 'jug go/_/yang de nyid las/_bcom ldan 'das chos thams cad mi mthong ba ni yang dag pa mthong ba'o zhes
[\[6b.5\]]gsungs so/_/de ltar chos thams cad rang bzhin med pa yin na 'jig rten mtha' dag nam mkha'i me tog dang 'dra bar 'gyur te/_de'i phyir mthong ba dang /_thos pa dang /_bye brag phyed pa dang /_'phags pa dang 'phags pa ma yin pa'i tha snyad la sogs pa med par 'gyur ro zhe na
[\[6b.6\]]klan ka 'di ni snying po yod pa ma yin te/_dngos po rnams kyi rang bzhin ni/_/rigs pa'i lam gyi rjes 'brang bar/_/gzhan dag 'dod pa sel bar byed/_/de phyir rgol ba ngan gnas med/_/yod dang med pa gang yang rung /_/khas mi len pa gang yin pa/_/sus kyang klan ka
[\[6b.7\]]bya mi nus/_/byis pa'i gnas skabs nas bzung ste thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi bar du snang ba nyams su myong ba gang ma brtags na nyams dga' ba'i dngos po ni kho bos bkag pa med de/_ser skya la sogs pas brtags pa gang yin pa de ni med do/_/de'i phyir chos thams cad rang
[\[7a\]]
[\[7a.1\]]bzhin med par smra ba 'di ni stong pa nyid kyi don log par mthong ba ma yin no/_/de phyir yang dag nyid du na/_/dngos po gang yang grub pa med/_/de phyir de bzhin gshegs rnams kyis/_/chos rnams thams cad ma skyes gsungs/_/dngos po rnams ni rnam
[\[7a.2\]]dpyad na/_/de dang de la gcig nyid med/_/gang la gcig nyid yod min pa/_/de la du ma nyid kyang med/_/yang dag par grub pa'i dngos po gang yang med de gcig dang du ma'i rang bzhin dang bral ba'i phyir ro/_/gcig dang du ma ma gtogs par/_/rnam pa gzhan dang ldan pa yi/_
[\[7a.3\]]dngos po mi rung 'di gnyis ni/_/phan tshun spangs te gnas phyir ro/_/de'i phyir na yang dag par na skye ba dang gnas pa dang 'gag pa yang yod par mi 'gyur ro/_/de lta bas na blo gros rgya mtshos bstan pa las gsungs pa/_gang dag rten cing 'brel 'byung ba/_/de dag dngos
[\[7a.4\]]nyid ci yang min/_/gang dag ngo bo nyid med pa/_/de dag gang du'ang 'byung ba med/_/ces gsungs so/_/glang po'i rtsal gyi mdo las kyang /_gang zhig skyes par gyur pa yi/_/chos de gang yang mi dmigs na/_/'byung ba med pa'i chos rnams la/_/byis pa dag ni 'byung
[\[7a.5\]]bar 'dod/_/ces gsungs so/_/yang smras pa/_bdag dang gzhan smras dngos 'di dag_/rang las ma yin gzhan las min/_/gnyis las ma yin rgyu med min/_/dngos po gang dang gang yang ni/_/skye ba nam yang yod ma yin/_/de ltar ma skyes ngo bo la/_/sus kyang klan
[\[7a.6\]]ka bya ru med/_/dkon mchog 'byung gnas kyi mdo las kyang /_gang la rang bzhin yod pa ma yin te/_/rang bzhin med pas gzhan rkyen ji ltar 'gyur/_/rang bzhin med pas gzhan gyis ji ltar bskyed/_/ces gsungs so/_/yab dang sras mjal ba'i mdo las kyang
[\[7a.7\]]gsungs pa/_chos gang la rang bzhin ma mchis pa de ni dngos po ma mchis pa'o/_/gang la dngos po ma mchis pa de yongs su ma grub pa'o/_/gang yongs su ma grub pa de ni mi skyed pa'o/_/gang mi skye ba de ni mi 'gag pa'o/_/gang ma skyes ma 'gags pa de ni 'das pa zhes bgyi bar
[\[7b\]]
[\[7b.1\]]gdags pa ma lags/_ma 'ongs pa dang da ltar byung ba zhes gdags par bgyi ba ma lags so/_/de ltar na don dam par ni dngos po dang dngos po med pa dang /_skye ba dang mi skye ba dang /_stong pa dang mi stong pa la sogs pa'i spros pa'i dra ba mtha' dag dang bral ba'o/_/de phyir
[\[7b.2\]]rtag chad lta ba rnams/_/gzhung 'di la ni ring du spangs/_/de yang kun rdzob kyi bden pa la brten nas ni rgyu mthun pa'i 'bras bu 'byung ste/_rgyu rnam par dag pa las ni 'bras bu rnam par dag pa 'byung ste/_dad pa dang /_'dun pa dang /_ngo tsha shes pa dang /_khrel yod pa dang /_
[\[7b.3\]]bag yod pa la gnas te/_sbyin pa nas shes rab kyi bar la slob pa dang /_bsdu ba'i dngos po dang /_tshad med pa dang /_sbyangs pa'i yon tan la nan tan byed pa dang /_dran pa nye bar gzhag pa dang /_yang dag par spong ba dang /_rdzu 'phrul gyi rkang pa la sogs pa la nan tan byed pa
[\[7b.4\]]ni 'khor los sgyur ba'i rgyal po dang /_tshangs pa dang /_brgya byin dang /_nyan thos kyi byang chub dang /_rang sangs rgyas kyi byang chub dang /_bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas thob par 'gyur te/_dper na sa bon grung po la sogs pa las 'bras bu 'byung ba bzhin no
[\[7b.5\]]zhes gsungs so/_/rgyu rnam par ma dag pa gang zhe na/_de yang bcom ldan 'das kyis rdo rje phreng ba'i rgyud las gsungs pa/_gsang ba pa'i bdag po nyon cig_/lus kyi nyes par spyod pa ni rnam pa gsum mo/_/ngag gi nyes par spyod pa ni rnam pa bzhi'o/_/yid kyi nyes par spyod pa
[\[7b.6\]]ni rnam pa gsum ste/_de dag gis sems can dmyal bar ltung bar 'gyur ro/_/phyag na rdo rjes gsol ba/_lus kyi nyes par spyod pa dang /_ngag gi nyes par spyod pa dang /_yid kyi nyes par spyod pa du zhig mchis pa bcom ldan 'das kyis bshad du gsol/_bde bar
[\[7b.7\]]gshegs pa bshad du gsol/_bcom ldan 'das kyis bka' stsal pa/_gsang ba pa'i bdag po nyes par spyod pa de nyid ni lci bar gyur ba dang tha mal pa rnams te/_de la pha dang /_ma dang /_bla mar gyur pa la sogs pa la gsod pa dang /_brdeg pa ni nyes par spyod pa lci ba'o/_/
[\[8a\]]
[\[8a.1\]]srog gcod pa la sogs pa mi dge ba'i las kyi lam rnams ni nyes par spyod pa tha mal pa'o/_/ngag gi nyes par spyod pa gang zhe na/_dam pa'i chos spong ba dang /_lha rnams la tshig rtsub mo smra ba dang /_pha ma dang bla mar gyur pa la sogs pa rnams
[\[8a.2\]]la tshig ngan pa smra ba ni ngag gi nyes pa lci ba'o/_/skyes bu 'ga' zhig gang zag dad pas nan tan nyams su len cing dge ba rtsom pa'i gtam gyi skabs de ni 'jig rten pha rol med do zhes bya ba'i rgya che ba'i tshig 'jig rten las 'das pa'i brdzun smra bas dge ba'i las kyi bar chad
[\[8a.3\]]byed pa dang /_tshig 'khyal pa smra ba dang /_lkog 'phyas byed pa dang /_mi dge ba'i las kyi lam gyi gtam rnams ni ngag gi nyes par spyod pa tha mal pa'o/_/yid kyi nyes par spyod pa ni bla ma dang /_pha dang ma dang theg pa chen po la zhugs pa'i sems can rnams yang dag par spong
[\[8a.4\]]ba la zhugs pa dang /_yang dag par rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas la ngan sems pa dang /_gnod par sems pa ni yid kyi nyes par spyod pa lci ba'o/_/dud 'gro la sogs pa tha mal pa'i sems can rnams la ngan sems dang gnod par sems pa ni tha mal pa'o zhes gsungs so/_/
[\[8a.5\]]de ltar 'bras bu ni rgyu'i rjes su 'jug pa'i phyir na dge ba la 'jug cing mi dge ba las ldog par bya'o/_/da ni ming la mngon par zhen pa rnams kyi 'khrul pa bsal ba'i phyir don dam pa'i bden pa'i ming gi rnam grangs 'ga' zhig la 'jug par bya ste/_de la dang po 'od gsal ba
[\[8a.6\]]dang /_thams cad stong pa dang /_dngos po med pa dang /_snang ba med pa dang /_bdag med pa dang /_mya ngan las 'das pa dang /_srog med pa dang /_gang zag med pa dang /_gso ba med pa dang /_skye ba med pa dang /_'gag pa med pa dang /_yi ge med pa dang /_tshig med pa dang /_
[\[8a.7\]]brjod du med pa dang /_bsam gyis mi khyab pa dang /_mtha' yas pa dang /_grangs med pa dang /_dbang po las 'das pa dang /_gnas med pa dang /_mtshan nyid med pa dang /_'dus ma byas pa dang /_mtshan ma med pa dang /_zad pa med pa dang /_sgrib pa med pa dang /_tshul
[\[8b\]]
[\[8b.1\]]gcig pa dang /_zhi ba dang /_nam mkha' dang mnyam pa dang /_rang bzhin gyis dag pa dang /_thog ma med pa dang /_dbus med pa dang /_tha ma med pa dang /_'gro ba med pa dang /_'ong ba med pa dang /_ring po ma yin pa dang /_nye ba ma yin pa ste/_de ltar rtogs par dka' ba'i
[\[8b.2\]]gnas so/_/de'i phyir gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud las kyang /_byang chub kyi sems ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi ye shes 'byung ba med pa'i gnas lta bu ste/_byang chub kyi sems de yang lus la mi gnas/_ngag la mi gnas/_sems la mi gnas so/_/chos gang
[\[8b.3\]]khams gsum na mi gnas pa de skye ba yang med/_'gag pa yang med pa ste/_'di ni ye shes 'byung ba'i gnas so zhes gsungs so/_/de ltar/_gzod nas zhi zhing ma skyes pa'i/_/rang bzhin dag pa'i chos nyid la/_/byis pa'i blo dang ldan pa rnams/_/yod dang med par rtog par
[\[8b.4\]]byed/_/ces gsungs so/_/de'i phyir byis pa so so'i skye bo thog ma med pa nas sgro 'dogs pa dang skur pa 'debs pas dkrugs shing log pa'i lta ba can gyis dag pa'i chos kyi dbyings 'od gsal ba'i don rtogs par dka' ba'i phyir na sgyu ma rnam par dag pa yid la bya'o/_/
[\[8b.5\]]phung po khams dang skye mched rnams/_/gzugs brnyan lta bur yongs shes na/_/yul gyi 'dom la mi chags so/_/de ltar yang shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa brgyad stong pa las gsungs pa/_rab 'byor gyis smras pa/_lha'i bu dag mya ngan las 'das pa yang rmi lam lta bu sgyu
[\[8b.6\]]ma lta bur nga smra'o/_/mya ngan las 'das pa las kyang ches lhag pa'i chos gzhan zhig yod kyang de yang sgyu ma lta bu rmi lam lta bu zhes gsungs so/_/de bzhin du rgyal ba skyed ma las kyang /_gzugs nas rnam pa thams cad mkhyen pa'i ye shes kyi bar du sgyu ma lta bu rmi lam lta bur
[\[8b.7\]]gsungs so/_/de ltar ye shes rdo rje kun las btus pa zhes bya ba rnal 'byor chen po'i rgyud las kyang gsungs pa/_sems dang sems las byung ba'i rnal 'byor chen po ni bde ba chen po'i ting nge 'dzin to/_/de ni sgyu ma'i dpes nye bar mtshon pa ste/_de bas na sangs rgyas kyi zhing
[\[9a\]]
[\[9a.1\]]gang+gA'i klung gi bye ma snyed kyi de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad ni sgyu ma lta bu dang /_chu zla lta bu dang /_mig yor lta bu dang /_smig rgyu lta bu dang /_rmi lam lta bu dang /_brag ca lta bu dang /_dri za'i grong khyer dang /_mig 'phrul dang /_'ja' tshon dang /_glog
[\[9a.2\]]dang /_chu'i chu bur dang /_me long gi gzugs brnyan te/_sgyu ma'i dpe bcu gnyis kyis bde ba chen po'i ting nge 'dzin nye bar mtshon par 'gyur ba yin te/_de ltar phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na gnas pa'i de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad 'khor ba ji snyed pa'i bar du sgyu ma
[\[9a.3\]]lta bu'i ting nge 'dzin gyis bzhugs nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing nas sangs rgyas kyi zhing du sems can gyi don mdzad do zhes gsungs so/_/dpal gsang ba 'dus pa'i rgyud las kyang gsungs pa/_kye bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad rmi lam 'di ni bdag gis khams
[\[9a.4\]]gsum du rmi lam mthong bar bya'o snyam du mi sems so/_/rmi lam yang bdag gis rmi lam mthong ngo snyam du mi sems te/_khams gsum gyi bya ba de rnams kyang rmi lam lta bu rmi lam dang 'dra ba rmi lam las byung ba'o/_/de bzhin du de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang byang chub
[\[9a.5\]]sems dpa' rnams dang sems can thams cad rmi lam lta bu bdag med pa'o/_/srog med pa'o/_/gang zag med pa'o zhes gsungs so/_/glang po'i rtsal gyi mdo las kyang /_shA ri'i bu 'di ji snyam du sems/_gang chos rnams kyi ngo bo nyid shes pa de yod pa yin nam/_'on te
[\[9a.6\]]med pa yin/_gsol pa/_bcom ldan 'das gang chos thams cad kyi ngo bo nyid 'tshal ba de ni sgyu ma'i ngo bo nyid 'tshal lo/_/de ci'i slad du zhe na/_bcom ldan 'das kyis chos thams cad sgyu ma ngo bo nyid do zhes bstan pa'i slad du ste zhes gsungs so/_/yab dang sras mjal
[\[9a.7\]]ba'i mdo las kyang /_me long yongs su dag pa la/_/ji ltar rang bzhin med pa yi/_/gzugs brnyan snang ba de bzhin du/_/ljon pa chos rnams shes par gyis/_/zhes gsungs so/_/rigs pa drug cu pa las kyang /_dngos po gzugs brnyan lta bur ni/_/ye shes mig gis
[\[9b\]]
[\[9b.1\]]rab mthong na/_/bdag nyid chen po de dag ni/_/yul gyi 'dam la mi chags so/_/zhes gsungs so/_/theg pa chen po nyi shu pa las kyang /_dngos po rnams kyi rang bzhin ni/_/gzugs brnyan dang ni mtshungs par 'dod/_/ces gsungs so/_/rin chen phreng ba las kyang
[\[9b.2\]]gsungs pa/_so so'i skye bo la gsang ba/_/gang yin de ni zab pa'i chos/_/'jig rten sgyu ma lta bu nyid/_/sangs rgyas bstan pa bdud rtsi yin/_/ji ltar sgyu ma'i glang po la/_/skye dang 'jig pa nyid snang yang /_/de la don gyis yang dag tu/_/skye dang 'jig pa nyid med ltar/_/de
[\[9b.3\]]bzhin sgyu 'dra'i 'jig rten la/_/skye dang 'jig pa nyid snang yang /_/dam pa'i don du skye ba dang /_/'jig pa nyid ni yod ma yin/_/ji ltar sgyu ma'i glang po ni/_/gang nas mi 'ong gang mi 'gro/_/sems rmongs tsam du zad pas na/_/yang dag nyid du gnas pa med/_/de bzhin sgyu
[\[9b.4\]]'dra'i 'jig rten ni/_/gang nas ma 'ongs gar mi 'gro/_/sems rmongs tsam du zad pas na/_/yang dag nyid du gnas pa med/_/ces gsungs so/_/de ltar phung po dang khams dang skye mched rnams ni sgyu ma'i rang bzhin te/_sgyu ma'i rnal 'byor yid la byed pa'i gang zag ni nyon mongs pa
[\[9b.5\]]med pa dang /_las dang /_sdug bsngal las grol bar 'gyur te/_rim gyis sgyu ma'i rang bzhin stong par shes pa 'byung ste/_de lta bas na chos thams cad sgyu ma lta bur yid la byas na ye shes sgyu ma lta bu nyid thob par 'gyur ro/_/de lta bas na lus dang ngag dang sems sgyu ma lta bus nyon
[\[9b.6\]]mongs pa dang las dang sdug bsngal sgyu ma lta bu las log la/_tshogs gnyis sgyu ma lta bu la 'jug na 'khor ba sgyu ma las thar bar byed pa 'di ni yang dag pa'i lam mo/_/de ltar na sgyu ma'i dpe brgyad dam bcu gnyis la brten te 'jug par bya'o/_/byis pa so so'i skye bo shes rab kyi mthu
[\[9b.7\]]chung ba rnams kyis lam ma nor bar 'jug pa'i rim pa dang /_lam gyi ngo bo mi shes pa rnams kyi don du bla ma dang mdo sde dang rgyud sde la brten nas gzhung du bkod pa'o/_/theg chen don bsdus sgron ma 'di/_/gzhung du bkod pa'i bsod nams des/_/'gro ba ma lus thams cad

[\[10a.1\]]dag//sku gsum myur du thob par shog_/theg pa chen po'i don bsdus pa'i sgron ma zhes bya ba/_slob dpon nag po zhabs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//_//rgya gar gyi mkhan po kr-iSh+Na ba de nyid dang /_lo tsA ba dge slong chos kyi shes rab kyis bsgyur cing zhus te
[\[10a.2\]]gtan la phab pa'o/_/[{D3721}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_gu ru pany+tsa biM shi ka_/bod skad du/_bla ma lnga bcu pa/_bcom ldan 'das rdo rje sems dpa' la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa'i gnas thob rgyur gyur pa/_/bla ma'i zhabs kyi pad+mar ji bzhin
[\[10a.3\]]btud byas te/_/de bstan pa ni dri med rgyud mang las gsungs pa/_/mdor bsdus bshad pa 'di ni gus pas mnyan par gyis/_/dbang bskur mchog thob rdo rje yi/_/slob dpon la ni de bzhin gshegs/_/phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten khams bzhugs pas/_/dus gsum du
[\[10a.4\]]ni mngon phyag 'tshal/_/mchog tu dad pas dus gsum du/_/dkyil 'khor me tog bcas thal mos/_/ston pa bla ma bsnyen bkur zhing /_/zhabs la spyi bos phyag bya'o/_/khyim pa'am ni gsar bu la/_/'jig rten smod pa spang ba'i phyir/_/dam chos la sogs mdun
[\[10a.5\]]bdar te/_/brtul zhugs 'dzin pas blos phyag bya/_/gdan bstabs pa dang ldang ba dang /_/don gyi bya ba sogs bsnyen bkur/_/brtul zhugs can gyis kun bya ste/_/phyag bya dam pa min las spang /_/bla ma dang ni slob ma dag_/mtshungs par dam tshig nyams 'gyur bas/_/
[\[10a.6\]]dpa' bos dang por slob dpon dang /_/slob ma'i 'brel pa brtag par bya/_/blo ldan slob mas bla mar ni/_/snying rje med cing khro la gdug_/khengs shing chags la ma bsdams dang /_/spyoms dang bcas par mi bya'o/_/brtan zhing dul la blo gros ldan/_/bzod ldan drang la g.yo
[\[10a.7\]]sgyu med/_/sngags dang rgyud kyi sbyor ba shes/_/snying brtser ldan zhing bstan bcos mkhas/_/de nyid bcu ni yongs su shes/_/dkyil 'khor 'dri ba'i las la mkhas/_/sngags bshad pa yi sbyor ba shes/_/rab tu zhi zhing dbang po dul/_/de 'dra'i mgon la bsams byas
[\[10b\]]
[\[10b.1\]]nas/_/slob mar gyur nas brnyas na ni/_/sangs rgyas thams cad brnyas pas na/_/des ni rtag tu sdug bsngal 'thob/_/slob dpon la ni smod pa de/_/yams dang 'tshe ba'i nad rnams dang /_/gdon dang rims dang dug rnams kyis/_/rmongs chen de ni 'chi bar 'gyur/_/

[\[10b.3\]]bar nges par 'tshed par 'gyur/_/mnar med la sogs 'jigs rung ba'i/_/dmyal ba bstan pa gang yin pa/_/slob dpon la ni smod pa rnams/_/der ni gnas par yang dag bshad/_/de bas 'bad pa thams cad kyis/_/rdo rje slob dpon blo gros che/_/dge ba rab tu
[\[10b.4\]]mi spyoms pa/_/nam yang smad par mi bya'o/_/bla ma la ni gus bcas yon/_/rjes su mthun par sbyin par bya/_/des ni rims sogs gnod pa rnams/_/phyir zhing 'byung bar mi 'gyur ro/_/rang gi dam tshig slob dpon ni/_/sbyin min bu dang chung ma dang /_/rang srog gis
[\[10b.5\]]kyang brten bya na/_/longs spyod g.yo ba smos ci dgos/_/gang phyir bskal pa bye ba ni/_/grangs med par yang rnyed dka' ba'i/_/sangs rgyas nyid kyang brtson ldan la/_/tshe 'di nyid la ster bar byed/_/rtag tu rang gi dam tshig bsrung /_/rtag tu de bzhin gshegs pa mchod/_/

[\[10b.7\]]nams tshogs yin te/_/tshogs las dngos grub mchog tu 'gyur/_/de bas slob ma snying rje gtong /_/tshul khrims bzod pa'i yon tan ldan/_/slob dpon dang ni rdo rje 'dzin/_/tha dad par ni mi brtag go/_/mchod rten bshigs 'dra'i sdig 'jigs pas/_/grib ma'ang bgom

[\[11a.1\]]par mi bya na/_/lham dang stan dang bzhon pa sogs/_/bgom mi bya ba smos ci dgos/_/blo gros chen po dga' sems kyis/_/bla ma'i bka' ni 'bad de mnyan/_/rigs pa yis ni mi nus pa/_/mi nus de la tshig gis sbyang /_/bla ma las ni dngos grub dang /_/

[\[11a.3\]]'gro dang /_/gtsug tor dag dang dpyangs pa dang /_/stan la rkang 'jog rked par ni/_/lag gzhag snye bar mi bya'o/_/bla ma dag ni langs pa na/_/nyal dang 'dug par mi bya'o/_/rtag tu de yi bya ba la/_/ldang mkhas phun sum tshogs par bya/_/mchil ma la sogs 'dor
[\[11a.4\]]ba dang /_/stan la rkang 'jog rkyong ba ni/_/'chag dang rtsod par smra ba dag_/bla ma'i mdun du mi bya'o/_/yan lag mnye dang gar dag dang /_/glu dang rol mo mi bya zhing /_/gtam gyi sbyor ba mang po rnams/_/thos pa'i nye 'khor du mi bya/_/btud de stan las ldang ba dang /_/gus
[\[11a.5\]]pa yis ni 'dug par bya/_/mtshan chu 'jigs bcas lam du ni/_/bsgo ba thob na mdun 'gro bya/_/slob dpon gyis ni mthong mdun du/_/blo dang ldan pas lus gcu dang /_/ka ba la sogs brten mi bya/_/sor mo'i tshigs ni drang mi bya/_/rkang pa bkru dang lus bkru dang /_/dril
[\[11a.6\]]dang mnye ba la sogs pa/_/phyag ni sngon du 'gro bas bya/_/de bzhin mthar ni ci bder bya/_/de yi mtshan smos brjod na ni/_/ming mthar zhal sngar ldan pas bya/_/gzhan dag gus par bya ba'i phyir/_/khyad par gyi ni tshig kyang brjod/_/bla ma la ni bka' stsal zhu/_/bka'
[\[11a.7\]]bzhin bgyid ces brjod byas la/_/thal mo sbyar zhing ma yengs par/_/bla mas bsgo ba mnyan par bya/_/dgod dang lud pa la sogs pa/_/lag pas kha ni dgab par bya/_/bya ba zin nas 'jam pa yi/_/tshig dag gis ni bzlas par bya/_/mdun du dul bar 'dug pa dang /_/
[\[11b\]]
[\[11b.1\]]gos sogs tshul bzhin bsdams pa dang /_/pus btsugs thal mo sbyar ba yis/_/mnyan sogs 'dod la gsol gsum gdab/_/bsnyen bkur spyod pa thams cad la/_/yid ni nga rgyal med par bya/_/ngo tsha 'jigs shing bsdams pa yis/_/bag ma gsar pa'i tshul
[\[11b.2\]]gnas bya/_/sgeg pa la sogs bya ba kun/_/ston pa'i mdun du spang bar bya/_/gzhan yang de 'dra'i bya ba ni/_/rang gis brtags la dor bar bya/_/rab gnas dkyil 'khor sbyin sreg dang /_/slob ma sdud dang 'chad pa rnams/_/yul der bla ma gnas pa na/_/rjes ma gnang
[\[11b.3\]]bar mi bya'o/_/spyan 'bye sogs las ci thob pa/_/de kun bla ma rnams la dbul/_/de yis bstabs pa blangs nas ni/_/gzhan dag la ni ci bder bya/_/bla ma'i slob ma slob mar min/_/slob ma'ang bla ma'i mdun du min/_/bsnyen bkur dag dang ldang ba dang /_/phyag sogs
[\[11b.4\]]byed pa bzlog par bya/_/slob dpon la ni gang 'bul dang /_/bla mas kyang ni gang stsal pa/_/de la btud de lag gnyis kyis/_/blo dang ldan pas blang bar bya/_/dran pa brjed med gyur pa dang /_/rang gi kun spyod la brtson pas/_/spun gyi rang spyod las 'das pa/_/dga'
[\[11b.5\]]bas phan tshun bzlog par bya/_/na bas bla ma'i bya ba la/_/btud de rjes ma gnang bar yang /_/bkag pa rnams ni spyad byas kyang /_/dge sems ldan la sdig mi 'gyur/_/'dir mang smra ba ci zhig dgos/_/bla ma dgyes byed gang yin bya/_/mi mnyes byed kun spang bar ni/_/de dang
[\[11b.6\]]de la 'bad de spyad/_/dngos grub slob dpon rjes 'brang zhes/_/rdo rje 'dzin pa nyid gsung bar/_/shes nas dngos po thams cad kyis/_/bla ma yongs su mnyes par bya/_/bsam pa dag pa'i slob ma ni/_/dkon mchog gsum la skyabs song la/_/bla ma'i rjes su 'jug pa
[\[11b.7\]]ni/_/kha ton bya bar sbyin par bya/_/de nas sngags sogs sbyin pa yis/_/dam chos snod du byas nas su/_/rtsa ba'i ltung ba bcu bzhi ni/_/klag dang 'dzin pa nyid du bya/_/de ltar bla ma'i rjes 'jug slob ma ni/_/ma lus phan bskyed skyon med 'di byas pa'i/_/dge ba mtha'
[\[12a\]]
[\[12a.1\]]yas bdag gis ci bsags pa/_/des ni 'gro kun myur du rgyal gyur cig_/bla ma lnga bcu pa slob dpon chen po rta dbyangs kyis mdzad pa rdzogs so//_//rgya gar gyi mkhan po pad+mA ka ra warma dang /_zhu chen gyi lo tsA ba dge slong rin chen bzang pos bsgyur cing zhus te
[\[12a.2\]]gtan la phab pa'o/_/[{D3722}]@##/_/rgya gar skad du/_gu rwA rA d+ha na pany+tsi ka_/bod skad du/_bla ma'i bsnyen bkur gyi dka' 'grel/_'jam pa'i rdo rje la phyag 'tshal lo/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi rang bzhin gyi/_/yon tan rnams kyi yon tan ldan/_/blar 'os bla
[\[12a.3\]]mar phyag byas nas/_/bla ma'i bsnyen bkur dka' 'grel brjod/_/de la 'dod pa'i lha gzhan dag gis ni mngon par 'dod pa'i 'bras bu grub par mi 'gyur bas/_brjod par bya ba la sogs pa nye bar bstan pas mchog tu 'dod pa sngon du 'gro ba'i sgrub pa la 'jug par bya ste/_mnyan par
[\[12a.4\]]bya zhes bya bas yid la bya ba slob dpon gyi gdams pa byin pa dang por re zhig de ston par byed pa'i tshigs su bcad pa/_dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa'i zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_de la 'di'i rkang pa dang pos ni dgos pa bstan to/_/gnyis pas ni 'dod pa'i lha la mchod pa bstan to/_/
[\[12a.5\]]gsum pa dang bzhi pa dag gis ni brjod par bya ba bstan pa yin la/_brjod bya dang rjod byed kyi mtshan nyid kyi 'brel pa ni gzhung gi khong na gnas pa nyid kyi phyir logs su ma gsungs so zhes bya ba ni spyi'i don to/_/yan lag gi don yang brjod par bya ste/_bla ma'i zhabs kyi pad+mar btud nas
[\[12a.6\]]zhes sbrel te/_bla ma'i zhes bya ba ni zab pa dang rgya che ba'i chos kyi man ngag sbyin pa'i phyir dang /_phan pa dang bde ba skyed par byed pa nyid kyis phar gyur pa'i phyir na mchod pa bkur sti la sogs pa rigs pas na bla ma yin la/_de'i zhabs kyang yin la pad+ma yang yin pas zhabs pad do/_/de
[\[12a.7\]]la btud nas ni phyag byas nas so/_/ji ltar zhe na/_de ni ji bzhin zhes bya bas bshad de/_cho ga'i rim pa las ma 'das pas ji ltar rigs pa ste/_lhag par dga' bas maN+Dal sngon du 'gro bas dul ba'i rnam 'gyur la sogs pa'o/_/de la 'di'i bla ma'i zhabs kyi pad+ma zhes bya bas ni
[\[12b\]]
[\[12b.1\]]bstod pa bstan la/_btud nas zhes bya bas ni phyag bya ba bstan to/_/'di dag gis ni mchod pa rnam pa gsum bstan te/_phyag bya ba ni lus kyi dang /_bstod pa ni ngag gi yin la/_lus dang ngag ni yid sngon du btang nas 'jug pa'i phyir yid kyi ni shugs kyis bstan to/_/'o na sangs rgyas la
[\[12b.2\]]sogs pa rnams 'dod pa'i lha yin mod/_ji ltar na bla ma rang gi 'dod pa dam pa yin zhe na/_'dir bla ma 'dod pa'i lha yin te/_lhag par byas pa nyid kyi phyir ram sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rang bzhin gyi sku yin pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/'chad par 'gyur ba
[\[12b.3\]]de lta'i mgon la bsam bcas pas/_/zhes bya ba la sogs pa'o/_/de bas na bla ma la mchod pa kho na grol ba'i byed pa po yin no/_/de ltar bla ma'i zhabs kyi pad+ma la phyag byas nas ci bya zhe na/_dri med ces bya ba gsungs te/_dri med ni rnam par dag cing skyon med pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/yang na/_
[\[12b.4\]]'di la mi dge ba'i dri ma yod pa ma yin pa ste/_dri ma yin pa ni dri ma dang bral ba'i rgyu'o zhes bya ba'i don to/_/'on kyang 'di dag rang gi yid kyi 'dod pa kho nas brtags pa ma yin nam zhe na/_de ma yin pa ni rgyud mang las gsungs pa zhes bya bas bshad de/_rgyud ni rgyun chags pa yin la/_
[\[12b.5\]]de yang rgyu la sogs pa'i dbye bas rnam pa gsum ste/_rgyu dang 'bras bu dang thabs zhes bya ba'o/_/de la rigs kyi dbye ba ni rgyu'i rgyud de/_rigs can gyi sems can rnams rab tu mang ba nyid kyi phyir rgyun chags par brjod do/_/rigs kyi dbye ba las 'bras bur gyur pa'i rdo rje 'chang chen
[\[12b.6\]]po'i dbye ba ni 'bras bu'i rgyud de/_mtha' yas pa'i sangs rgyas kyi chos kyi rang bzhin yin pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/rgyu las 'bras bu 'grub pa'i ched du sngags dang phyag rgya dang dkyil 'khor la sogs pa'i rkyen rnams ni thabs kyi rgyud de/_sngags dang phyag rgya la sogs pa'i thabs chen po
[\[12b.7\]]rnams kyi cho ga dpag tu med pa'i phyir ro/_/de yang gtso bo nyid kyi dbye bas cho ga mang po ste/_bya ba dang /_spyod pa dang /_rnal 'byor dang /_rnal 'byor bla ma dang /_rnal 'byor bla na med pa'i rgyud ces bya ba de dag thams cad du 'brel pa rnams so/_/rgyud mang po de dag tu gsungs shing bshad
[\[13a\]]
[\[13a.1\]]pa ni rgyud mang las gsungs pa'o/_/'o na bcom ldan 'das nyid kyis de dang de las gsungs pa'i phyir 'di brtsams pa la dgos pa med do zhes bya bar dogs pa la/_mdor bsdus nas bshad par gsungs te/_rgyud mang po lta bas 'jigs pa'i skye bo rnams la phan
[\[13a.2\]]pa'i phyir rgyud mang po las/_lus pa med par phyung nas gcig tu bsdus te 'dir mngon par brjod pa yin no zhes bya bar dgongs so/_/'di zhes pa ni 'dod pa'i bla ma bsten pa rgyas par bshad pa'o/_/de ltar 'di zhes pa ni de nyan pa la skal ba dang ldan pa'i sems can rnams sbyar bar bya ba'i
[\[13a.3\]]phyir mnyan par gyis zhes bya ba gsungs te/_mnyan par gyis ni rna ba spags la'o/_/de zhes pa ni lhag ma'o/_/ji lta bu zhe na/_gus pas zhes bya ba gsungs te/_gus pa ni 'dir nyan pa'i tshul te/_phyin ci ma log pas yi ge dang don 'dzin pa dang dad pas yang dag par 'dzin pa yin
[\[13a.4\]]pas khyed cag gis bla ma las mnyan par gyis shig ces bya bar sbyar ro/_/rnam pa gzhan du khas sbubs pa dang mi gtsang ba dang rdol ba'i bum pa la sogs pa rnams su char bab pa lta bur don dang bral ba nyid yin pas de'i gtam mi bya ba'i phyir ro/_/gang gi ched du 'di gus pas mnyan par
[\[13a.5\]]bya zhe na/_dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' zhes bya ba gsungs te/_dpal ni bsod nams kyi tshogs dang ye shes kyi tshogs gsum la skyabs su 'gro ba la sogs pa bsod nams dang /_don dam pa'i byang chub kyi sems bsgom pa la sogs pa ye shes kyi tshogs so/_/pha rol tu phyin pa'i tshul gyis
[\[13a.6\]]na sbyin pa dang tshul khrims dang bzod pa gsum ni bsod nams kyi tshogs yin la/_shes rab dang thabs dang smon lam dang ye shes dang stobs kyi pha rol tu phyin pa lnga ni ye shes kyi tshogs so/_/brtson 'grus kyi pha rol tu phyin pa dang bsam gtan gyi pha rol tu phyin pa ni gnyi gar gtogs so/_/rdo rje
[\[13a.7\]]sems dpa' zhes pa la/_mi phyed pa nyid kyis rdo rje dang chos mthun pas rdo rje yin la/_mi 'jig cing nyams par mi 'gyur bas sems dpa'o/_/rdo rje yang 'di yin la sems dpa' yang yin pas rdo rje sems dpa' ste/_rang bzhin gyis 'od gsal zhing rang bzhin gyis rtag pa nyid kyis
[\[13b\]]
[\[13b.1\]]rtag pa'i rdo rje 'dzin pa'o zhes bya ba'i don to/_/yang na chos thams cad la khyad par 'gro ba'i phyir na rdo rje ste chos kyi dbyings yin la/_de la rtag par rab tu 'jug pa nyid kyi phyir rdo rje sems dpa' de nyid do/_/nges pa'i tshig gis yi ge rnams phyis pa dang bstan pa yang yin no/_/dpal dang ldan
[\[13b.2\]]pa'i rdo rje sems dpa' ni dpal ldan rdo rje sems dpa' ste/_bar gyi tshig phyis pa'i bsdu ba'o/_/de'i go 'phang ni rdo rje sems dpa'i gnas te rdo rje 'chang nyid do zhes bya ba'i don to/_/de thob pa ni brnyes par gyur pa ste/_de'i rgyu ni byed pa de las so/_/'o na de mnyan pa tsam gyis 'dod pa'i don
[\[13b.3\]]grub pa'i rgyur 'gyur ram zhe na/_bden mod kyi 'on kyang brgyud pas 'gyur ba kho na ste/_'di ltar de thos nas bya ba dang bya ba ma yin pa yongs su shes la/_de dag las ni tshogs so/_/de las kyang 'dod pa'i don grub pa'i rgyur 'gyur ba yin no/_/de'i phyir bla na med pa'i 'bras bu'i don du bla
[\[13b.4\]]ma bsten pa mnyan nas gus pa dang bcas pas brtson par bya ba yin la/_de ston par byed pa'i gzhung la yang de skad ces bya ste/_rol rnyed ma 'phrogs pa'i snyan ngag bzhin no/_/mchog tu 'dod pa'i lha la mchod pa dang brjod par bya ba la sogs pa'i don gyi tshigs su bcad pa nye bar bkod
[\[13b.5\]]nas/_dbang bskur mchog ces bya ba la sogs pas slob dpon gyi che ba'i bdag nyid bstan pa gsungs te/_rdo rje'i slob dpon la ni de bzhin gshegs/_/rnams la phyag 'tshal zhes sbrel lo/_/rdo rje ni rdo rje 'chang gi brtul zhugs yin la/_de kun du spyod pa'i phyir rdo rje'i slob dpon no/_/
[\[13b.6\]]yang na gzhan dag 'byed par byed cing gzhan dag gis dbye bar bya ba ma yin pas rdo rje dang chos mthun pa'i phyir gnyis su med pa'i ye shes ni rdo rje yin la/_de la slob ma rnams 'dzud par byed cing kun du spyod par byed pas na rdo rje'i slob dpon no/_/de ji lta bur gyur pa zhig ce na/_dbang
[\[13b.7\]]bskur zhes gsungs te/_dbang bskur ni khrus yin la/_de yang phyi lus kyi dri ma 'khrud par byed pa'i phyir dbang bskur zhes brjod par bya'o/_/mchog ni gtso bo ste bla na med pa'i 'bras bu 'thob pa'i rgyu yin pa nyid kyi phyir ro/_/dbang bskur ba yang yin la/_mchog kyang 'di yin pas
[\[14a\]]
[\[14a.1\]]dbang bskur mchog go/_/yang na dbang bskur ba rnams kyi mchog ni rtse mo ste mthar thug pa'i bzhi pa zhes bya ba ni dbang bskur mchog go/_/de dag gis thob pa de ni dbang bskur mchog thob bo/_/ni ni gang gi phyir gyi don la'o/_/yang na kho na dang rigs pa la'o/_/de
[\[14a.2\]]bzhin gshegs pa ni bgrod par bya ba ji lta ba de lta bu kho nar gshegs pas na de bzhin gshegs pa ste/_dus thams cad dang /_rnam pa thams cad dang /_shes bya thams cad yang dag par mkhyen pa'i phyir ro/_/ngo mtshar la kha cig tu ldog pas na/_ta yig da yig ste/_bsam pa
[\[14a.3\]]ji lta ba dang /_rigs ji lta ba dang /_dus ji lta bar gdul bya'i skye bo rnams la yang dag pa'i chos ston par mdzad pa'i phyir ji skad du gsung bar 'os pa de skad du gsung bas de bzhin gshegs pa ste/_de bzhin gshegs pa de rnams kyis so/_/ji lta bur gyur pa de rnams kyis she na/_phyogs
[\[14a.4\]]bcu'i zhes gsungs te/_bcu ni shar la sogs pa bzhi dang /_me la sogs pa bzhi dang /_steng dang 'og gnyis te/_de ltar phyogs kyang yin la bcu yang yin pas phyogs bcu'o/_/'jig rten khams zhes bya ba ni yongs su dag pa dang yongs su ma dag pa'i sangs rgyas kyi zhing 'phags
[\[14a.5\]]pa dang 'phags pa ma yin pa rnams te/_'jig rten 'dzin par byed do zhes byas nas so/_/phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams de dag na bzhugs pa ste phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams na gnas pa de rnams kyis so/_/dus gsum zhes bya ba ni dus gsum po rnams te/_snga dro dang gung
[\[14a.6\]]dang phyi dro'i dus rnams su zhes bya ba'i don to/_/de rnams nas byon nas phyag 'tshal ba ni mngon phyag 'tshal ba ste 'dud pa zhes bya ba'i don to/_/'o na slob dpon gyis de bzhin gshegs pa rnams la phyag bya ba ma yin nam/_de la ji ltar na de rnams kyis 'di la phyag mdzad ce na/_rdo rje 'chang
[\[14a.7\]]gi sku yin pa'i phyir dang /_rdo rje 'chang de yang de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi bdag nyid yin pa'i phyir te/_slob dpon dang ni rdo rje 'dzin/_/tha dad par ni mi brtag go/_/zhes 'chad par 'gyur ba yin no/_/dpal 'dus pa las gsungs pa/_byis pas gsol pa/_bcom
[\[14b\]]
[\[14b.1\]]ldan 'das rnams de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyi sku dang gsung dang thugs rdo rje gsang ba 'dus par dbang bskur ba'i rdo rje'i slob dpon la de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis ji ltar blta bar bgyi/_de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad kyis bka'
[\[14b.2\]]stsal pa/_rigs kyi bu de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad dang byang chub sems dpa' thams cad kyis byang chub kyi sems rdo rje bzhin du blta bar bya'o zhes bya ba la sogs pa le'u bcu bdun pa las rgya cher gsungs so/_/de bzhin gshegs pa rnams kyis rdo rje'i slob dpon la phyag mdzad do
[\[14b.3\]]zhes bya ba 'di la mkhas pa rnams kyis som nyi mi bya'o/_/de ltar slob dpon mnyes par byed pa'i cho ga de rab tu bsdus nas dus gsum zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa yin te/_bsten pa zhes bya ba dang 'brel lo/_/de zhes bya ba ni dbang bskur ba mchog thob pa'i rdo rje'i slob dpon
[\[14b.4\]]no/_/bsten pa zhes bya ba ni yang dag par mnyes par byed pa'o/_/de ci 'dra ba zhig ce na/_ston pa bla ma zhes bya ba ste/_sems can rnams la mngon par mtho ba dang nges par legs pa'i lam gyi man ngag ston pa'i sgo nas ston pa po yin pa'i phyir ston pa ste slob pa po'o/_/yon tan gcig
[\[14b.5\]]pu'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir bla ma'o/_/ci zhig gis she na/_dkyil 'khor me tog thal mos zhes bya ba gsungs te/_dkyil 'khor ni snying po yin la/_de len zhing 'dzin pas na snying po yang dag par 'dzin pa'i maN+Dal rnams te/_pha rol tu phyin pa drug bsdus pa'i rang bzhin yin
[\[14b.6\]]pa'i phyir chu dang bcas pa'i ba byung sbyin pa ste zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs pa ltar ro/_/maN+Dal ni zlum po'i rnam pa'am gru bzhi'i rnam pa gang yang rung ba chu dang ba byung la sogs pa rnams byugs pa'o/_/ma l+li ka la sogs pa'i me tog rnams ni me tog yin la/_thal mo ni lag pa kha
[\[14b.7\]]sbyar ba ste/_me tog rnams kyi thal mo ni me tog thal mo'o/_/me tog thal mo dang dkyil 'khor rnams ni dkyil 'khor me tog thal mo ste de rnams so/_/yang ci zhig gis she na/_zhabs la ste rkang pa dag la phyag 'tshal zhing mngon par 'dud par bya ba de rnams kyis so/_/spyi bo ni spyi
[\[15a\]]
[\[15a.1\]]gtsug ste zhabs la spyi bos so/_/ji ltar zhe na/_mchog tu zhes bya ba gsungs te/_ji ltar rigs pa de lta bu'i gus pas bsten zhing bsnyen pa na dam par nges pa dang /_rgya chen po nyid kyis zhes bya ba'i don to/_/ci nas gcig gam zhe na/_dus gsum du
[\[15a.2\]]zhes bya ba gsungs te/_thun mtshams gsum mo/_/ji ltar zhe na/_me tog dang bcas pa'i snyim pa bskor ba las zhes bya ba ni me tog dang bcas pa'i thal mo ni bya ba'i khyad par ste me tog gi snyim pa zhes bya ba'i don to/_/'o na bstan pa'i rtsa ba dge slong ste zhes gsungs pa'i phyir bcom ldan
[\[15a.3\]]'das kyi bstan pa la dge slong rnams tshad ma ma yin nam/_de la ci ltar na slob dpon la bsnyen par mngon par brjod ce na/_de rnams tshad ma yin pa ni theg pa dman pa kho na la yin gyi theg pa chen po la ni ma yin no/_/de bas na slob dpon thams cad du mnyes par byas pa kho nas bstan pa
[\[15a.4\]]yin no/_/yang dpung bzang gi rgyud du/_rgyal bas so so thar par gang gsungs pa'i/_/tshul khrims rnam dag 'dul ba ma lus la/_/khyim pa'i rtags 'chang rnams kyis rtags drug gis/_/g.yogs pa spangs nas lhag ma bsgrub par bya/_/zhes gsungs so/_/dge slong tshul
[\[15a.5\]]khrims sdom pa kun/_/'dzin pas gos dkar 'chang ba la/_/phyag mi bya'o phyag gi 'os/_/rdo rje 'dzin gtso rang nyid do/_/gang nas brtsams te dag pa'i yid kyis ni/_/ma nyams byang chub sems ni bzung gyur pa/_/de nas bzung ste lha dang lha min bcas/_/'jig rten kun gyi phyag bya'i
[\[15a.6\]]'os yin no/_/de bas bdag nyid legs pa yi/_/don 'dod dam pa rnams kyis ni/_/mtha' yas 'bras bu rtsol mdzad pa'i/_/slob dpon dngos po kun gyis so/_/rdzogs pa'i byang chub nges byas pa/_/rnams kyis phrag dog ser sna dang /_/nga rgyal ngar 'dzin dor bya zhing /_/g.yo
[\[15a.7\]]dang sgyu yang de bzhin no/_/rtag tu ngu yis mi 'dar ba'i/_/sems kyis slob dpon bsnyen bkur bas/_/'gro ba'i mgon po bla ma yis/_/don kun grub pa stsal ba'o/_/de lta bas na rdo rje'i slob dpon zhes bya ba yang dag par mnyes par bya'o/_/da ni bla ma bsten pa thun mong ba bstan nas
[\[15b\]]
[\[15b.1\]]dge slong rnams la ji ltar bya ba de/_de lta bur bstan par bya ba'i phyir dam chos zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_brtul zhugs 'dzin pas khyim pa'am gsar bu la phyag bya zhes sbrel te/_bstan bcos su rnam par bzhag pa'i sdom pa ni brtul zhugs te rab tu byung ba nyid do/_/de
[\[15b.2\]]'dzin par byed pa'i phyir brtul zhugs 'dzin pa rnams te/_gsol ba dang bzhis lnga'i tshogs kyis bsnyen par rdzogs pa blangs pa yongs su rdzogs pa'i tshul khrims kyi sdom pa 'jig rten gyis mchod par bya ba ngur smrig gi gos can dge slong rnams zhes bya ba'i don to/_/de skad du yang bshad
[\[15b.3\]]pa/_gang zhig tshul khrims legs mnyam gzhag_/de la ngur smrig dang ldan te/_/bden dang dul ba dang ldan pa/_/de nyid mchod 'os ngur smrig yin/_/zhes gsungs so/_/gzhan du na ming gi dge slong dang khas 'che ba'i dge slong dang slong ba'i ngang tshul gyi dge slong rnams brtul zhugs
[\[15b.4\]]'dzin pa'i sgras brjod par mi bya'o/_/tshul khrims la ni mnyam ma bzhag_/de la ngur smrig mi ldan te/_/bden dang dul dang mi ldan pa/_/de ni mchod 'os ngur smrig min/_/zhes so/_/gang la phyag bya ba yin zhe na/_khyim pa'am ni gsar bu la'ang /_/zhes bya ba gsungs te/_
[\[15b.5\]]'di la khyim yod pa'i phyir khyim pa ste/_khyim gyi nang na gnas shing phyag gi gnas ma yin pa 'dod pa'i yon tan la zhen pa khyim gyi gnas zhes bya ba'i don to/_/gsar bu zhes bya ba ni/_/rab tu byung ba gsar pa ste dge tshul lo/_/'am gyi sgra ni phyogs gzhan pa gnyis la'o/_/'ang
[\[15b.6\]]gi sgra ni brjod pa'i dbye ba la'o/_/phyag bya zhes pa ni 'jig rten gyis mchod par 'os pa rnams kyis te bdag cag rnams ni dge slong gnas brtan no snyam pa'i nga rgyal spangs nas mngon par phyag bya'o/_/ji ltar byas nas she na/_dam chos la sogs zhes bya ste/_sems can rnams
[\[15b.7\]]ngan 'gror phyogs pa las 'dzin par byed pa'i phyir chos so/_/dam pa sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyi chos ni dam pa'i chos so/_/yang na 'di 'jig rten las 'das pa'i phyir dam pa yin la/_rang gi mtshan nyid 'dzin pa'i phyir chos yin pas dam pa'i chos te/_
[\[16a\]]
[\[16a.1\]]de yang lung dang rtogs pa dang /_chos kyi dbyings te rnam pa gsum mo/_/de la lung ni gsung rab yan lag dgu'o/_/rtogs pa ni sa dang pha rol tu phyin pa rnams dang /_nyon mongs pa'i sgrib pa dang shes bya'i sgrib pa spangs pa dag go/_/chos kyi dbyings dang
[\[16a.2\]]de bzhin nyid dang yang dag pa'i mtha' dang don dam pa zhes pa dag rnam grangs so/_/de dag ston par byed pas na glegs bam la de skad ces brjod par bya'o/_/dam chos la sogs te thang ka dang sku gzugs gang gi dang po yin pa de dag ni dam chos la sogs pa'o/_/de rnams mdun
[\[16a.3\]]bdar nas zhes bya ba ni sngun du bkod pa ste mdun du bzhag nas zhes bya ba'i don to/_/de nas ci zhe na blos te bsam pa'am shes rab kyi stobs kyis so/_/'o na dge slong gi phyag bya ba ni sangs rgyas dang sngar bsnyen par rdzogs pa gnyis kho na yin par/_phyag bya gnyis te bde gshegs rgan
[\[16a.4\]]po'o/_/zhes de skad du gsungs pa ma yin nam zhe na/_bden mod kyi/_de skad du gsungs pa ni nyan thos kyi tshul la yin gyi phyi nas byang chub sems dpa'i tshul la ni ma yin la/_'di ni byang chub sems dpa'i tshul yin zhing bye brag tu sngags kyi tshul yin te de bas na skyon med do/_/yang na sangs
[\[16a.5\]]rgyas kyi sgras ni sangs rgyas 'ba' zhig bsdus pa ma yin gyi/_byang chub sems dpa' rnams kyang bsdus la/_rgan po'i sgras kyang bsnyen par rdzogs pas rgan pa 'ga' zhig bsdus pa ma yin gyi/_ye shes kyis rgan pa dang dka' thub kyis rgan pa yang bsdus pa yin no/_/rnam pa
[\[16a.6\]]gzhan du na 'phags pa byams pa dang 'jam dpal la sogs pa'i byang chub sems dpa' khyim na bzhugs pa'i rtags can rnams phyag bya ba'i 'os ma yin par 'gyur ro snyam du dgongs so/_/de bas na tshig 'di dag ni nyan thos kyi theg pa dang yang 'gal ba med do/_/dgongs pa'i
[\[16a.7\]]skad ni mi shes par/_/sgra tsam gyis ni rmongs pa dag_/rgyal dbang rnams kyi so thar la/_/smad pa byas nas ngan 'gror 'gro/_/zhes gsungs pa yang yin no/_/de bas na rdo rje'i slob dpon khyim pa'am gsar bu la dge slong gis kyang rnam pa thams cad du phyag bya ba yin no/_/de
[\[16b\]]
[\[16b.1\]]skad du kye'i rdo rje'i rgyud las/_slob ma gang gis grub thob kyang /_/mnar med spang ba'i rgyu yi phyir/_/yang dag ye shes snang mdzad pa'i/_/bla mar grub pas phyag bya'o/_/zhes so/_/gal te de ltar yin nam/_dam pa'i chos la sogs pa mdun du byas pa la dgos pa ci yod ce
[\[16b.2\]]na/_/'jig rten gnod pa zhes bya ba gsungs te/_'jig rten pa rnams la gnod pa ni 'jig rten gnod pa ste 'gro ba sun 'byin par byed pa de dag spong zhing nyams par byed pa de'i phyir ni 'jig rten gnod pa spang ba'i phyir ro/_/'o na rang gi bla ma la phyag bya ba la 'jug pa rnams kyis
[\[16b.3\]]'jig rten la gnod pa yod dam zhe na yod do/_/ji ltar yod ce na/_'jig rten phal mo che 'di ni bstan bcos ma thos shing ma rig pa'i phyir don dam pa'i chos la gnas pa yongs su mi shes so/_/de las de rnams kyis slob dpon dge slong nyid du gyur pa bsnyen bkur pa'i 'os ma
[\[16b.4\]]yin par yid la byed do/_/de bas na de rnams kyis khyim pa la phyag byas pas rab tu byung ba rnams sun 'byin par byed la/_sun phyung bas 'jig rten rnams phyir phyogs par 'gyur ro/_/'jig rten phyir phyogs pas kyang 'jig rten las rnyed pa dang bkur sti nyams par byed do/_/ma
[\[16b.5\]]dad pa na rnyed pa dang bkur sti sdug bsngal bas 'tshol/_sdug bsngal ni 'jig rten na mthar gyur pa yin no/_/rnyed pa dang bkur sti dang mi ldan pa la sogs pa'i 'jig rten la gnod pas 'jigs pas phyag byed pa na dam pa'i chos la sogs pa mdun du bdar ba la don med pa ma yin no/_/
[\[16b.6\]]gal te na yang ci bya ba bstan pa'i phyir stan bstabs pa dang zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_brtul zhugs can gyis thams cad bya/_/zhes sbrel lo/_/brtul zhugs can ni brtul zhugs 'dzin pa yin la/_bya ba ni nyams su blang ba'o/_/thams cad ces bya ba de dag gang la
[\[16b.7\]]bya zhe na/_stan bstabs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa yin no/_/'di la 'dug par bya bas na stan te/_ma sU ra ka la sogs pa'i gdan no/_/de bstabs pa ni dang po dbul ba yin la/_ldang ba ni de'i don du nan tan byed pa'o/_/yang na ldang ba ni yang dag par ldang ba ste/_'grengs
[\[17a\]]
[\[17a.1\]]te 'dug pa zhes bya ba'i don to/_/stan yang stobs la ldang ba yang yin pas stan bstabs pa dang ldang ba'o/_/yang gsungs pa/_ma dang pha dang bla ma la/_/su zhig ldang bar mi byed pa/_/'jig rten kun gyis smod 'gyur bas/_/tha shal dag dang mtshungs par
[\[17a.2\]]'gyur/_/zhes so/_/don bya zhes bya ba la don te rdzas kyi bya ba byed pa ni don bya yin la/_skyed 'phel yang don no/_/de la skyed ni gtong ba la sogs pas yin la/_'phel ni tshong la sogs pas so/_/sogs pa'i sgras ni bsrung ba la sogs pa yang ngo /_/yang na don zhes bya ba ni gos
[\[17a.3\]]dang stan la bya la/_bya zhes bya ba ni nan tan no/_/sogs pa'i sgras ni bangs pa dang mchil ma dang snabs 'dor ba la sogs pa la sgrib pa'o/_/bsnyen bkur zhes pa ni bla ma la gus shing dad pas zhes bya ba'i don te/_don gyi bya ba sogs pa gang gi yin pa de ni don gyi bya ba sogs te/_de ni
[\[17a.4\]]don gyi bya ba sogs kyang yin la bsnyen bkur yang yin pas don gyi bya ba sogs bsnyen bkur ro/_/yang na tshig 'di dag rim pa bsnor nas so/_/yang na don yang byed la/_bsnyen yang bkur bas don gyi bya ba sogs bsnyen bkur ro/_/thams cad nyid ni ma lus par te/_nyid kyi sgra
[\[17a.5\]]ni nges par gzung ba'o/_/'di dag thams cad byas nas brtul zhugs can gyi nga rgyal med par bya'o zhes dgongs so/_/yang gsungs pa/_de bas nges pa kho nar ni/_/brtul zhugs brten pas 'di kun bya/_/de bzhin nang dang phyi yis ni/_/rtag par rnal 'byor mchod la dga'/_/
[\[17a.6\]]phyag sogs bya ba thams cad dag_/dus rnams kun du bya ba yin/_/de ltar yongs su brtags nas ni/_/bla ma rnams la bsnyen bkur bya/_/'on kyang /_gzugs dang lang tsho phun tshogs dang /_/longs spyod dbang phyug dag dang stobs/_/skye dang rigs rgyud mi bsam ste/_/nga
[\[17a.7\]]rgyal dag ni dor bar bya/_/bzo yi cha shas 'di kun la/_/blo dang ldan zhing mkhas snyam dang /_/bdag ni sa skyong dge ba'o zhes/_/sems la sbyar bar mi bya'o/_/zhes so/_/ci byas nas she na/_dam pa min las phyag spong ngo /_/zhes bya ba gsungs te/_sku dang gsung dang
[\[17b\]]
[\[17b.1\]]thugs la gnod pa'i las ni dam pa min pa zhes bya ste/_mi mdzes pa'i phyag ni sdig pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir ro/_/de dam pa min pa yang yin la/_las kyang yin pas dam pa min las te/_srog gcod pa la sogs pa'i mi dge ba zhes bya ba'i don to/_/de la stan bstabs pa la
[\[17b.2\]]sogs pa 'di dag thams cad nam gyi tsha na bya ba yin zhe na/_phyag byas nas zhes bya ba gsungs te/_gus par smras nas so/_/dam min phyag gi las zhes bya bar 'don pa de la ni/_las kyang yin la phyag kyang yin pa ste/_de dam pa min pa yang yin la phyag gi las kyang yin pas
[\[17b.3\]]na dam min phyag gi las so/_/dam pa ma yin pa ni bshad zin te/_dam pa ma yin pa'i phyag ni ma gus pa sngon du song bar nges par mtshon pa'i thal mo sbyor ba tsam byed pa'o/_/yang na dam pa ma yin pa tha mal pa'i skye bo rnams kyi phyag gi la ste/_de ni lo ma rnying pa lhags shing 'bras
[\[17b.4\]]bu 'bab pa'i khur gyis dud pa'i rnam par sbyong ba la sogs pa dam pa ma yin pa'i las te/_mgo bo dud pa tsam ni dam min phyag go/_/gzhan dag ni/_dam min las dang phyag ces bya ste/_dam pa ma yin pa'i las rkang pa bkru ba la sogs pa dang /_yan lag brgyad kyis
[\[17b.5\]]btud pa'i phyag ste gnyis po 'di dag spangs nas bya ba thams cad bya'o zhes so/_/de ltar bla ma'i rab tu dbye ba bshad nas slob dpon zhes bya ba la sogs pas/_bla ma dang slob ma dag yongs su brtag par gsungs te/_slob dpon dang slob ma'i 'brel ba bya zhes bya ba la
[\[17b.6\]]'brel ba'i dang por te sngon du'o/_/nye ba'i dbang las slob ma ste bla ma ni slob dpon zhes bya ba bla ma dang ni slob ma dag go/_/slob dpon dang slob ma de dag gi 'brel pa ni 'grogs pa ste/_slob dpon dang /_slob ma'i 'brel pa brtag par bya ni dpyad par bya'o/_sus
[\[17b.7\]]snyam na/_dpa' bos zhes bya ba gsungs te/_blo dang ldan zhing mkhas pa rnams kyis zhes bya ba'i don to/_/'di'i don ni 'di yin te/_bla mas re zhig cha lugs dang /_brjod pa dang /_spyod lam la sogs pa rnams kyis ci 'di bsam
[\[18a\]]
[\[18a.1\]]pa dag pa yin nam/_bsam pa ma dag pa yin snyam du yongs su brtag par bya zhing /_ci 'di brtsam par bya ba'am mi bya snyam du dang /_de'i khyim gyi mtshams na gnas pa'i skye bo rnams la 'di'i bya ba yongs su dris shing brtags nas ci 'di la shog
[\[18a.2\]]cig bya'am/_mi bya snyam du dpyod pa'i tshul gyis kyang yongs su brtag par bya'o/_/de lta bu la sogs pa rnams kyis yongs su brtags na 'jig rten pa'i bsam pa shes par 'gyur te/_cha byad rtags dang spyod lam dang /_/skad kyis kyang ni rtogs bya zhing /_/mig dang gdong gi
[\[18a.3\]]rnam 'gyur gyis/_/nang na gnas pa'i bsam pa shes/_/zhes kyang gsungs so/_/de yongs su brtags pa la dgos pa ci yod ce na/_'jig rten phal mo che ni bsam pa yongs su ma dag pas bla ma la sri zhu byas pa med par de kho na nyid 'dod pas rgyal po ltar kun du spyod de/_
[\[18a.4\]]de skad du/_sgyu yis dri mar byas pa'i sems/_/ngan pa'i bsam pas 'bul byed cing /_/gtan du bla ma bsnyen bkur yang /_/bkur sti med cing phyag kyang min/_/mnyam par gzhag pa thob pa'i bar/_/'o ma la sogs 'bul bas mchod/_/sangs rgyas kun gyi yon tan
[\[18a.5\]]gzhi/_/de nyid rin chen thob pa na/_/bzhugs sam zhes kyang mi 'dri la/_/skyon nyid rtag tu tshol bar byed/_/ces so/_/de bas na de ltar yang dag par brtags nas bsam pa yongs su dag par gyur na de'i tshe de dang 'brel par bya ba yin gyi/_de lta ma yin na ni mi bya'o zhes
[\[18a.6\]]dgongs so/_/de bzhin du slob mas kyang yongs su brtags nas bla ma dang lhan cig pa'i 'brel pa bya'o/_/de ci'i phyir zhe na/_'jig rten phal mo che ni bsam pa ma dag pas kho bo cag ni slob dpon no zhes bcos ma'i tshig snyan po dang 'di'i don sna tshogs pa la chags pas dam pa
[\[18a.7\]]min pa'i chos ston pas sam/_tshul 'chos pa'i gtam gyis sems can rnams slu bar byed do/_/de bas na slob mas kyang ci 'di bsam pa dag pa yin nam/_bsam pa ma dag pa yin snyam du bla ma yongs su brtag par bya ste/_gal te bsam pa ma dag na de'i tshe de dang lhan cig
[\[18b\]]
[\[18b.1\]]pa'i 'brel pa mi bya'o/_/yang gsungs pa/_bla mar bya ba min par bshad/_/log pa'i shes rab mngon par khengs/_/chags pa'i dbang gis gzhan dag la/_/chos ston pa yang rab tu 'jug_/byis pa de dag sems can gyi/_/mi dge'i bshes gnyen de dag ni/_/bdud
[\[18b.2\]]kyi phyogs dang ris su gnas/_/rang dang gzhan dag nyams byed pa/_/de dag rtag par sems can gyis/_/spang zhing bsnyen bkur bya ba min/_/de rnams la ni phyag mi bya/_/kun du myang bar yang mi bya/_/zhes so/_/de bas na bsam pa ma dag pas ming tsam gyi slob dpon ni
[\[18b.3\]]legs pa 'dod pa rnams kyis rnam pa thams cad du yongs su spang bar bya'o/_/gal te bsam pa ma dag pa'i slob ma'am bla ma lhan cig pa'i 'brel pa byas pa de'i tshe gnyis ka la cir 'gyur/_/spyod pa ma yin pa las dam tshig nyams par 'gyur ro/_/dam tshig nyams
[\[18b.4\]]par gyur na de la cir 'gyur zhe na/_mtshungs pa zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_mtshungs pa ni mnyam pa'o/_/dam tshig ni slob dpon gyis 'gong bar bya ba ma yin pa'o/_/de dam tshig kyang yin la mtshungs pa yang yin pa'i phyir mtshungs pa dam tshig ste mtshungs pa
[\[18b.5\]]nyid ni gnyis ka yang 'di'i bya ba'i rang bzhin yin pa'i phyir ro/_/rnam pa gnyis po de yang bsrung bar bya ba dang bza' bar bya ba'o/_/de la bsrung bar bya ba yang rnam pa gnyis te/_blang bar bya ba dang /_dor bar bya ba'o/_/de la blang bar bya ba ni dge ba'i rang bzhin rnams dang /_
[\[18b.6\]]dor bar bya ba ni mi dge ba'i rang bzhin rnams so/_/blang bar bya ba yang rnam pa gsum ste/_lus dang ngag dang yid kyi'o/_/de la srog gcod pa la sogs pa ni lus kyi'o/_/brdzun du smra ba la sogs pa ni ngag gi'o/_/brnab sems la sogs pa ni yid kyi'o/_/bza' ba'i dam
[\[18b.7\]]tshig kyang rnam pa gnyis te/_rtag tu nye bar spyad pa dang /_skabs su nye bar spyad pa'o/_/de la rtag tu nye bar spyad pa ni sgron ma lnga la sogs pa'o/_/skabs su nye bar spyad pa ni rdo rje bzung ba la sogs pa'o/_/yang na mtshungs pa'i dam tshig ces bya ba la mtshungs pa ni 'dra ba ste/_
[\[19a\]]
[\[19a.1\]]mnyam pa dang mthun pa zhes bya bar gcig pa'i don to/_/dam tshig gi don tshig rnam par sbyar ba ni snga ma bzhin no/_/mtshungs pa'i dam tshig de yang rnam pa gnyis te/_bla ma'i bya ba dang /_slob ma'i bya ba'o/_/de la slob ma'i bya ba ni cho ga ji lta ba bzhin
[\[19a.2\]]dbang nod pa'o/_/de nas brtsams te khyod kyi phyag na rdo rje nga yin gyi gang ngas 'di bya dgos so/_/sngags dang phyag rgya dang dkyil 'khor la sogs pa 'di dag kyang khyod kyis dbang bskur ba ma thob cing dkyil 'khor ma mthong ba rnams la smra bar mi bya ste/_ya nga ba ma spangs par dus kyi bya
[\[19a.3\]]ba byas nas dmyal ba la sogs par 'gyur ta re zhes bya ba la sogs pa brjod par byed pa ni bla ma'i bya ba'o/_/bla ma la sogs pa mtho ba rnams kyi yang dag pa'i spyod pa gang yin pa de slob ma'i bya ba'o/_/mtshungs pa'i dam tshig nyams pa ni 'khyams pa'o/_/mtshungs pa'i dam tshig
[\[19a.4\]]nyams pa de yang skyon te/_ltung ba dang mi dge ba zhes bya ba'i don to/_/hi ni gang gi phyir gyi don la'o/_/su'i skyon du 'gyur zhe na/_slob dpon dag ces bya ba gsungs te/_slob dpon dang slob ma ni dpon slob ste de dag gi'o/_/dgongs pa ni 'di yin te/_dam tshig nyams na
[\[19a.5\]]slob dpon gyi dngos grub nyams pa'i rgyu yin pa'i phyir skyon yin la/_slob ma'i yang 'dir lus dang sems gzir ba'i nye bar 'tshe ba skyed par byed pa'i phyir dang /_phyi ma la yang ngan 'gro'i sdug bsngal skyed par byed pa'i phyir na skyon chen po ste/_de bzhin du dam pa ma yin pa'i kun du spyod
[\[19a.6\]]pa yang yin no/_/slob ma'i skyon bstan pa'i phyir/_brtse ba med ces bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_bla mas slob mar mi bya'o/_/zhes 'brel lo/_/bla ma ni bshad zin la/_bslab pa la slob pas na slob ma ste slob bu'o/_/de la mi bya ba mi sgrub pa'o/_/bla ma ji lta bus she na/_
[\[19a.7\]]blo ldan zhes bya ba la blo ni blo gros dri ma med pa yin la/_de 'di la yod pa'i phyir blo ldan no/_/slob ma'i khyad par ci 'dra ba zhig ce na/_brtse ba med ces bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_sdug bsngal dang sdug bsngal gyi rgyu las 'don par 'dod pa'i mtshan nyid kyi snying rje ni brtse ba yin
[\[19b\]]
[\[19b.1\]]la/_de las 'das pa gang gis na brtse ba med pa de ni brtse ba med do/_/khro ba ni khong khro zhing 'khrug pa ste mi bzod par gyur pas 'phral du gnod pa byed pa zhes bya ba'i don te de ni khro ba'o/_/gdug pa ni sems rtsub mo ste/_brtse ba med pa zhes bya ba'i don to/_/khengs pa
[\[19b.2\]]ni cung zad kyis dregs pa zhes bya ba'i don to/_/chags pa ni pha rol gyi rdzas 'dod pa'o/_/ma bsdams pa ni g.yo zhing mnyam par ma bzhag pa'o/_/bkag par gyur pa ni bdag nyid mchog yin no zhes bdag nyid bsngags shing gzhan la smod pa ste/_tshul khrims 'di
[\[19b.3\]]la bdag mchog tu gyur pa'o zhes bya bar ro/_/gsungs pa/_mchog yin zhes ni rab smra ba'i/_/yon tan rnams ni sbyin par byed/_/ces so/_/dang yig ni kun bsdus pa'i don to/_/dang yig las 'di lta bu dag ni bla mar yang mi bya'o zhes ni gzhan dag go/_/bla ma'i rang
[\[19b.4\]]bzhin bstan pa'i phyir/_brtan zhing zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_bsam pa dang blos shin tu zin pa'i phyir bstan pa ste blo dang ldan pa'o/_/dul ba ni 'dul ba bzhin du'o/_/blo gros ni rnam par dpyod pa ste shes rab yin la de 'di la yod pa'i phyir blo gros ldan pa ste rnam par
[\[19b.5\]]dpyad pa zhes bya ba'i don to/_/bzod pa ni bzod par gyur ba ste/_de yang sdug bsngal la ji mi snyam pa'i bzod pa dang /_gzhan gyi gnod pa dang du len pa'i bzod pa dang /_chos la nges par rtog pa'i bzod pa dang rnam pa gsum mo/_/de lta bu'i mtshan nyid kyi bzod pa gang la yod pa
[\[19b.6\]]de ni bzod ldan no/_/drang ba ni 'phags pa'i sa la rab tu bzhugs pa'i phyir gya gyu med pa'i lta ba can te/_gya gyu ni sdig pa can gyi lta ba'o/_/gya gyu ci yin sdig can lta/_/zhes gsungs pa'o/_/g.yo sgyu med pa ni rang gi skyon sgrib pa'i thabs kun du 'dzin pa'i sems kyi gya gyu nyid g.yo
[\[19b.7\]]yin pas de la zhugs pa ni g.yo ste/_g.yo dang bral zhing g.yo med la gya gyu med pa'i sems zhes bya ba'i don to/_/sngags rgyud kyi ni rab sbyor shes te sngags ni shes pa ste/_de kho na nyid kyi don yid la byas pas 'gro ba skyob pa'i phyir na sngags so/_/de yang phreng ba'i sngags dang
[\[20a\]]
[\[20a.1\]]btus pa'i sngags dang snying po'i sngags zhes bya ba rnam pa gsum mo/_/rgyud ni phyir bzlog gi 'khor lo la sogs pa'o/_/sngags dang rgyud ni sngags rgyud de/_/de rnams kyi rab sbyor ni zhi ba la sogs pa'i las te/_de shes pa'i phyir sngags rgyud kyi ni rab sbyor
[\[20a.2\]]shes pa'o/_/snying rjer ldan pa ni sems can thams cad la snying rje ba dang ldan pa'o/_/bstan bcos mkhas pa ni 'chos pa'i phyir bstan bcos te/_gzhung du spel ba yin la/_/de yang mdor bsdu na rnam pa bcu gnyis te/_chos dang /_rtog ge dang /_don dang /_sgra dang /_gar
[\[20a.3\]]dang /_ro bcud dang /_yongs su brtag pa dang /_'dod pa dang /_gso ba dang /_rtsis dang /_bzo dang /_rnam par shes pa'i bstan bcos dag go/_/bstan bcos la mkhas pa ni 'chos pa la mkhas pa'o/_/slar yang slob dpon gyi khyad par bstan pa'i phyir/_de nyid
[\[20a.4\]]bcu zhes bya ba la sogs pa gsungs te/_bcu ni rab tu grags pa'i grangs te bgrang ba la 'jug go/_/de nyid ni phyin ci ma log pa'i rang bzhin no/_/de rnams de nyid kyang yin la bcu yang yin pas na bcu'i grangs su 'chad pa'i de nyid dag ni de nyid bcu'o/_/de nyid bcu po dag kyang
[\[20a.5\]]dkyil 'khor dang /_ting nge 'dzin dang /_phyag rgya dang /_sngags dang /_stang stabs dang /_'dug stangs dang /_bzlas pa dang /_sbyin sreg dang /_mchod pa'i las la sbyor ba dang /_slar bsdu ba dag go/_/dkyil 'khor yang rnam pa gsum ste/_sku'i dkyil 'khor dang /_gsung
[\[20a.6\]]gi dkyil 'khor dang /_thugs kyi dkyil 'khor ro/_/ting nge 'dzin ni rnam pa gsum ste/_dang po sbyor ba dang /_dkyil 'khor rgyal po mchog dang /_las rgyal po mchog rnams ngo bo nyid dang /_longs spyod rdzogs pa dang sprul pa'i sku'i dbye bas so/_/phyag rgya ni rnam pa gnyis te/_
[\[20a.7\]]lag pa'i phyag rgya dang /_yid kyi sku'i phyag rgya'o/_/sngags ni bshad zin to/_/stang stabs ni rnam pa mang ste/_bung ba'i dra ba la sogs pa'o/_/'dug stangs ni mdor bsdus na rnam pa bzhi ste/_pad+ma'i 'dug stangs dang rdo rje'i 'dug stangs dang sems dpa'i 'dug stangs dang khro
[\[20b\]]
[\[20b.1\]]bo'i 'dug stangs so/_/bzlas pa ni rnam pa bzhi ste/_khro bo'i bzlas pa dang rdo rje'i bzlas pa dang spro ba'i bzlas pa dang 'gog pa'i bzlas pa'o/_/sbyin sreg ni rnam pa bzhi ste/_zhi ba dang rgyas pa dang dbang dang mngon spyod do/_/mchod pa'i las la sbyor ba ni/_phyi nang gsang
[\[20b.2\]]ba'i mchod pa'i nan tan la rab tu sbyor ba'o/_/slar bsdu ba ni rnam pa gnyis te/_ye shes kyi dkyil 'khor gshegs su gsol ba dang dam tshig gi dkyil 'khor bsdu ba'o/_/de nyid bcu po rnams yongs su shes shing khong du chud pas ni de nyid bcu ni yongs su shes pa'o/_/dkyil
[\[20b.3\]]'khor bri ba'i las la mkhas/_/dkyil 'khor ni bri bya'i dkyil 'khor te ri mor bri ba'i dkyil 'khor dang /_bri ba ni dkyil 'khor bri ba ste de dag gi las ni bya ba yin la/_de dag rig cing shes pa'i phyir dkyil 'khor bri ba'i las la mkhas pa'o/_/de la dkyil 'khor
[\[20b.4\]]gyi las ni phyi dang nang gi sa sbyang ba dang yongs su gzung ba dang /_bgegs la phur bus gdab pa dang /_phyogs bcing ba dang /_mtshams bcing ba dang /_lha lhag par gnas pa dang /_thig dang rdul tshon gdab pa dang /_bum pa lhag par gnas shing dgod pa dang /_
[\[20b.5\]]dkyil 'khor sgrub pa la sogs pa'o/_/bri ba'i las kyang snam bu dang dar dpyang dang 'khor lo la sogs pa bri ba'o/_/gsang sngags 'chad byed nam oM yig la sogs pa de kho na nyid gsum ro gcig pa'i gsang chen gyis bshad par bya ba'i sngags rnams 'chad pa la mkhas
[\[20b.6\]]shing rtogs pa'i phyir gsang sngags 'chad byed de/_yang gsungs pa/_sngags dang sngags shes rab gsungs pa/_/de nyid bskul bar gsungs pa ste/_/skye ba med cing snang ba med/_/mtshon bya dang ni mtshan nyid spangs/_/'di la sngags zhes brjod pa yin/_/gsang chen
[\[20b.7\]]don ni rtogs pa yin/_/zhes so/_/slob dpon zhes bya ba ni/_dbang bskur ba la sogs pa'i las la 'jug pa'i phyir slob dpon te/_yang gsungs pa/_chos kyi kha ton klog pa dang /_/'chad dang man ngag sbyin pa dang /_/dbang bskur ba dang las byed pa/_/slob dpon zhes
[\[21a\]]
[\[21a.1\]]byar brjod pa yin/_zhes so/_/dang ba zhes pa ni ser sna dang bral zhing snying nas dga' ba'o/_/dang yig las ngo bzhin gsal ba'o/_/dbang po thul zhes bya ba la gang gis mig la sogs pa'i dbang po rnams dbang du byas nas thul ba de ni dbang po thul ba'o/_/ba'ang zhes bya ba
[\[21a.2\]]ni lhag par sdud pa'o/_/slob dpon la smod pa'i skyon/_mgon de zhes bya ba la sogs pas gsungs te/_de zhes bya ba ni de lta bu'i yon tan gyis khyad par du byas pa'i slob dpon gang yin pa de'o/_/mgon zhes pa ni sangs rgyas dang byang chub sems dpa' la sogs pa rnams kyi mgon
[\[21a.3\]]du gyur cing mnyes par bya ba yin pa'i phyir mgon te mgon de'o/_/gang gis zhes bya ba ni slob mar rmongs pas so/_/brnyas pa ni smod par byas pa'o/_/cir gyur nas she na/_slob gyur phyi nas zhes gsungs te/_slob ma ma yin pa las slob mar gyur nas zhes
[\[21a.4\]]bya ba slob gyur phyi nas so/_/bsam bcas pas ni bsam pa dang lhan cig tu 'jug pas bsam bcas te bsam pa thag pa nas yin gyi smyo ba'am ma shes pa'am rnam par g.yengs pa'i sems kyis ni ma yin pa'o/_/sangs rgyas thams cad smod pas na sangs rgyas ni de
[\[21a.5\]]bzhin gshegs pa rnams te/_chos thams cad kyi don dam pa thugs su chud pa'i phyir sangs rgyas yin pa'am/_'di dag dri ma med pa'i blo can yin pa'i phyir sangs rgyas so/_/yang na dus thams cad mkhyen cing skyon thams cad dang bral bas na yang dag par rlom pa'i
[\[21a.6\]]seng ge dang 'phrog byed dang dbyig gi snying po la sogs pa'i lha rnams pas rgyas shing thugs su chud pa'i dgongs pa dang ldan pa'i phyir sangs rgyas rnams so/_/thams cad ni ma lus pa ste/_phyogs bcu'i 'jig rten gyi khams ji srid par bzhugs pa de dag thams cad do/_/de dag
[\[21a.7\]]ni sangs rgyas kyang yin la thams cad kyang yin pas sangs rgyas thams cad de sangs rgyas de dag thams cad la brnyas shing smod la 'phya ba des ni sangs rgyas thams cad la smod pa yin no/_/de ni zhes pa ni su zhig bla ma la brnyas pa byed pa 'di de'o/_/rtag tu ni rgyun du'o/_/
[\[21b\]]
[\[21b.1\]]sdug bsngal ni nye bar 'joms pa ste/_da yang 'di pa dang 'jig rten pha rol pa rnam pa gnyis so/_/de la mthong ba'i chos la lus dang sems gzir ba nye bar 'tshe ba la sogs pa rnams ni 'di pa'o/_/dmyal ba la sogs pa rnams su gcod pa dang gshegs pa dang sreg pa
[\[21b.2\]]dang 'tshod pa la sogs pa'i sdug bsngal rnams ni 'jig rten pha rol pa'o/_/'thob ces bya ba ni myang bar bya zhing nyams su myong dgos so zhes bya ba'o/_/slob dpon ni de kho na nyid thugs su chud pas sangs rgyas zhes de skad du brjod pa de ni sangs rgyas thams cad kyi rang
[\[21b.3\]]bzhin yin pas na de la smod pa las sangs rgyas thams cad smad pa las skyes pa'i sdug bsngal 'byung ba yin no/_/de gang las she na/_slob dpon ni de bzhin gshegs pa thams cad lta bur blta bar bya'o zhes pa'i bcom ldan 'das kyi gsung tshad ma yin pa'i phyir ro/_/yang
[\[21b.4\]]gsungs pa/_/brtan g.yo'i 'jig rten gsum po na/_/slob dpon las mchog bla ma med/_/gang gi drin las dngos grub kun/_/'phral nyid du ni thob par byed/_ces so/_/slar yang bla ma smod pa'i nyes dmigs bye brag tu bstan pa'i phyir yams dang nyer 'tshe zhes bya ba
[\[21b.5\]]gsungs te/_bla ma'i zhabs la smod pa 'chi bar 'gyur ro zhes 'brel lo/_/bla ma ni slob dpon yin la/_de'i zhabs ni zhabs dag ste de dag la smod cing sun 'byin pa ni bla ma'i zhabs la smod pa'o/_/'chi bar 'gyur ba ni 'chi ba'i 'os te rnam par nyams par 'gyur ro zhes bya ba'i don to/_/ci
[\[21b.6\]]zhig dag gis she na/_de'i phyir/_yams dang nyer 'tshe dgra rnams kyis/_/zhes bya ba gsungs te/_yams ni rdo rje'i me 'bab pa dang chu dang rlung dang mu ge dang gshed ma la sogs pa rnams kyis gzir bar byas pa'o/_/nyer 'tshe ni 'byung po dang yi dgas dang 'dre dang srin po dang
[\[21b.7\]]sbrul dang gcan gzan gtum po la sogs pa las byung ba'i nye bar 'tshe ba rnams so/_/dgra ni sha 'khon can gyi dgra rnams so zhes bya ba'i don to/_/yams dang nye bar 'tshe ba dang dgra rnams te yams dang nyer 'tshe dgra rnams kyis so/_/dang yig las gnyan rnams kyis kyang
[\[22a\]]
[\[22a.1\]]ngo /_/yang gang dag gis she na/_gdon dang rims zhes bya ba gsungs te/_gdon ni nyi ma la sogs pa'i gza' dgu po dag gam yang na ma mo la dga' ba la sogs pa bcu gnyis po dag ste/_sems can rnams kyi mdangs dang stobs len par byed

[\[22a.3\]]mdor bsdu na brtan pa dang g.yo ba dang bcos ma dang gyur pa ste rnam pa bzhi'o/_/de la brtan pa ni nag po brtsegs pa la sogs pa'o/_/g.yo ba ni sbrul la sogs pa rnams kyi'o/_/bcos ma ni kun du sbyar ba dag go/_/gyur ba ni rnam par rtog pa las byung ba'o/_/sogs pa'i

[\[22a.5\]]chen po yang yin pas rmongs chen te shin tu blun pa'o/_/de ltar shes nas legs pa 'dod pa dag gis slob dpon la smod par mi bya bar yon tan kho na gzung bar bya'o/_/yang gsungs pa/_slob dpon yon tan gzung bya ste/_/skyon ni nam yang ma yin no/_/yon tan gzung bas
[\[22a.6\]]dngos grub ste/_/skyon rnams las ni grub pa nyams/_/zhes so/_/slar yang rgyal po zhes bya ba la sogs pas bla ma la smod pa'i rnam par smin pa gsungs te/_bla ma'i zhabs la smod pa zhes sbyar nas bsad nas dmyal bar 'gro zhes sbrel lo/_/bsad nas ni shi nas dmyal ba na
[\[22a.7\]]'gror 'gro zhing 'bor bar byed do/_/su dag gis bsad nas she na/_rgyal gtum zhes bya ba ste/_rgyal po ni sa skyong ba yin la/_gtum po ni mdzod spung ba dang /_dum bu srung ba la sogs pa rnams te/_rgyal po dang gtum po ni rgyal gtum mo/_/yang na rgyal po ni rnam thos
[\[22b\]]
[\[22b.1\]]kyi bu la sogs pa gsang ba pa'i gtso bo rnams te 'dir rgyal po'i sgras ni gsang ba rnams so/_/gtum po ni gsheg par byed pa dang /_gzir bar byed pa rnams te/_rgyal po dang gtum po ni rgyal gtum gnod sbyin gyi mngag gzhug pa rnams zhes bya ba'i don to/_/me ni me nyid
