[\[94b.4\]]'khor ni/_/chos 'dzin rigs kyi grub gnas su/_/thugs rjes sa la mngon sprul gshegs/_/byang chub sems kyi dkyil 'khor mchog_/byams mgon dam pa zhig gis bstan/_/e ma khyed kyis ma shes sam/_/mthun yun kun du bde ba yin/_/sgron mes mun khung gser tshol ltar/_/gsang
[\[94b.5\]]ba'i snying po mdzod brtol te/_/thig le gcig gis kun la khyab/_/thams cad lung chen nges par bstan/_/'jig rten g.yo rdul mi yi rang bzhin rnams/_/'bar ba lnga bcu'i khro bo ngang du snang /_/mya ngan 'das dang 'khor ba'i rang bzhin rnams/_/btsal med ma bcos de nyid rnam dag
[\[94b.6\]]nas/_/thig le nyungs kar tsam zhig gsal bar bsgom/_/de las 'od zer rdul snyed spros/_/mun gsal dngos po kun sbyangs te/_/thams cad ma bcos sku ru gsal/_/slar 'dus thig le la thim nas/_/'od du zhu nas rim gyis bsdus/_/rdo rje sems dpa'i snying gi nang /_/a gzugs
[\[94b.7\]]pad+ma 'dab bzhir gnas/_/de steng gsang ba nang gnas sa rlung dang /_/snying ga nang gnas chu rlung gnyis/_/rnam par dge las zla ba ste/_/rdo rje rin chen gnyis rang bzhin/_/de steng rdo rje sems dpa' ni/_/thig le 'od zer lnga ldan pas/_/de steng mgrin gnas me rlung dag_/mgo bo'i nang
[\[95a\]]
[\[95a.1\]]gnas rlung dkyil gnyis/_/dag pas nyi ma'i dkyil 'khor steng /_/pad+ma'i rigs dang las rigs so/_/kha sbyar dbus su thig le bsam/_/yang dang yang du 'dris bsams pas/_/yar 'gro mar 'gro gnyis 'gog go/_/'gog pa bzhin du mtshan ma ste/_/laM skye 'gag
[\[95a.2\]]med pa'i chos nyid kyi rnam par snang ba'i sgo'o/_/maM mi zad pa chos nyid rnam par snang ba'i sgo'o/_/paM gnyis skyon med pa chos nyid rnam par snang ba'i sgo'o/_/taM thogs pa med pa chos nyid rnam par snang ba'i sgo'o/_/muM brjod pa las 'das pa'i chos nyid rnam par snang ba'i sgo'o/_/hUM mi g.yo ba'i chos
[\[95a.3\]]nyid yongs su snang ba'i sgo'o/_/oM cir yang snang ba'i chos nyid rnam par snang ba'i sgo'o/_/sa ni chu la thim pas ni/_/kun du mnyam bros zag med pa'i/_/las kyi ye shes dang por skye/_/chu ni me la thim pas na/_/sems la dbang thob du ba 'dra/_/me ni rlung la thim pas na/_/ting 'dzin 'ba'
[\[95a.4\]]zhig ldan pa ste/_/rlung gi rnam pa lta bur mthong /_/rlung ni rnam par rig pa la/_/thim pas 'dod pa rnams bral te/_/mar me lta bur mthong ba'o/_/rnam par rig pa'i 'od gsal la/_/thim pa thams cad snang ba ni/_/phyi nang mun pa thams cad sbyangs/_/nam mkha' lta bur mthong ba'o/_/e
[\[95a.5\]]ma'o dngos po med pa las/_/smon dang snying rje'i dbang gis ni/_/ji ltar snang ba ma bkag pa'o/_/'dun pa'i dus na rigs kyi bu/_/yid la byed pa zhes thob ste/_/sems gsum bskyed cing mtha' bcu grol/_/brten pas gzhi yi sa par gnas/_/rigs chen 'byed pa'i rnal 'byor la/_/'phro
[\[95a.6\]]'du gcig pa'i ting 'dzin thob/_/sems bzhi rdzogs te mtha' bcu shes/_/bdag nyid yi ge'i phreng bar ni/_/snang ba'i ltas mthong bsod nams gter/_/dbugs chen 'byin pa'i rnal 'byor la/_/sems gcig rdzogs te mtha' chub nas/_/'jigs pa lnga yang khyad par sa/_/yongs su
[\[95a.7\]]mi ldog ting 'dzin sa/_/'jig rten nor bu rin chen gyis/_/gang bar spyod pa'i ltas mthong 'gyur/_/sgyu ma sbyor ba'i skyes bu ste/_/'khor los sgyur ba'i cha byad du/_/rin chen bdun dang dpung tshogs kyis/_/dbang bsgyur thabs kyi theg pa ston/_/lung chen thob pa'i skabs su ni/_/seng ge dag la
[\[95b\]]
[\[95b.1\]]zhon nas ni/_/thams cad gnon pa'i ltas mthong 'gyur/_/sems bdun rdzogs pa'i sa par gnas/_/'bras bu nyid la lam shes pas/_/lam gyi yan lag bde rdzogs te/_/gzhan dag smin par bya ba'i phyir/_/ji ltar 'dod ltar thabs mchog sbyor/_/rtsal chen rdzogs pa'i skabs su ni/_/
[\[95b.2\]]kun snang ting 'dzin nyid thob ste/_/des ni nyi zla'i cha bskor bas/_/thabs dang gsal bar byed ltas mthong /_/sems gsum bskyed cing mtha' drug chub/_/gdeng du gyur pa'i ngo bo las/_/de nas rgyal mtshan skyes bu de/_/chos kyi rgyal po gang de yi/_/gdung 'tshob dga' ldan theg chen ston/_/
[\[95b.3\]]mi gnas bcu dus cho 'phrul snang /_/bshes gnyen dam pas bka' stsal pa/_/sa bcu pa la gnas pa yang /_/chos nyid du 'jog spyod par byed/_/mi rtog ngang du mi gnas te/_/rdzogs pa'i sangs rgyas mi byed do/_/e ma skyes bu dam pa klong /_/gang gis ngo bo ci phyir lags/_/skyes bu
[\[95b.4\]]dam pas bka' stsal pa/_/gsang sngags dngos po brgyad kyis bcings/_/mnyam par ma bzhag bar du ni/_/sangs rgyas dgongs pa myong ma yin/_/skyes bu dam pa khyod ci gu/_/gang zhig mos pa su zhig gis/_/ji ltar grol 'gyur ngo bo ci/_/skyes bu dam pas bka' stsal pa/_/grol bar
[\[95b.5\]]'dod pas bla ma bsten/_/rigs pa rang byung rang bzhin ni/_/byang chub sems kyi dkyil 'khor ro/_/bsod nams tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor ni/_/zhing khams rin chen yod pa na/_/rgyal ba kun du bzang po yi/_/sras mchog 'jam dpal chen po la/_/ji ltar rim gyis brgyud pa bzhin/_/de
[\[95b.6\]]bzhin 'byor pa'i yo byad la/_/rnam gsum tshul du nan tan bya/_/bsod nams tshogs kyi dkyil 'khor ro/_/bka' stod pho nya'i dkyil 'khor ni/_/sangs rgyas mi bskyod pa yi ni/_/zhing khams mngon par dga' ba na/_/rgyal tshab skyes bu kun gyis gsungs/_/de yi gdams ngag mdor bkod
[\[95b.7\]]pa'o/_/rtags dang rten ni gzhung ltar bsham/_/dur khrod chen po rab 'jigs pa'i/_/mtsho ni rkong rkang thang dmar na/_/ri ni byin lag mchongs kyi rtse/_/steng na 'dab chags rgyal po gnas/_/keng rus thod pa mkhar du brtsigs/_/ru las tshogs bdag bskyed nas ni/_/nye gnas kro ti shwa
[\[96a\]]
[\[96a.1\]]ri ma/_/rang gi 'khor tshogs ldan pa bskyed/_/de nas dpa' bo chen po yi/_/ru lu hUM gi 'od zer spros/_/drag po'i gnas nas gdug pa dgug_/zhal du rngubs te sna nas bton/_/gzhon nu sme brtsegs zhes gyur te/_/bskyed dang gnyis su med par byas/_/de la ming
[\[96a.2\]]dang mtshan btags pa/_/gang gi rgyal po zhes kyang bya/_/lha chen legs ldan nag po ste/_/lha yi sde dpon ka ru na/_/tshogs bdag chen po bdud kyi rje/_/dge slong thar pa nag po yin/_/tshogs bdag chen po de gsol la/_/dpa' bo chen po gshegs su gsol/_/bdag cag skal ldan
[\[96a.3\]]'dus pa'i tshogs/_/sgo 'dir 'jug par 'tshal lags na/_/rgyal ba'i sras su gzung du gsol/_/dpa' bo chen pos bka' stsal pa/_/hUM hUM hUM bi shwa badzra kro ta badzra maN+Dal phaT/_ta keM ta keM phaT/_/ha la ha raM/_tig sna tig sna khaM/_kro ta kro ta yaM/_oM hUM muM/_skal ldan 'dus pa'i tshogs
[\[96a.4\]]chen khyed/_/bde bar 'ongs so legs par 'ongs/_/grub pa'i rlung sgo gsang sgo 'dir/_/su dag 'ongs pa slar mi ldog_/tshogs bdag chen pos yang gsol pa/_/bdag cag mtha' yas sems can rnams/_/don gyis sangs rgyas yin mod kyang /_/rtog pa'i dbang gis 'khor ba la/_/byang
[\[96a.5\]]chub mchog tu sems bskyed do/_/sems nyid sangs rgyas yin pa la/_/mun pas bsgribs pas de mi shes/_/byang chub sems kyi lam 'di nas/_/sangs rgyas sa la 'jug par bgyis/_/dpa' bo chen pos bka' stsal pa/_/rdo rje can gyi rnal 'byor khyod/_/rdo rje can du cig nges na/_/gsang
[\[96a.6\]]ba gsum du mnyam pa nyid/_/mi phyed rdo rje dam tshig sbyin/_/mi phyed rdo rje'i dam tshig ni/_/gsang ba gsum gyi dbyings nas byung /_/dkyil 'khor gsum gyi dam tshig ni/_/grub na 'jigs pa'i dus med do/_/nag po chen pos yang gsol pa/_/ye shes rin chen dbu rgyan mchog_/gzi brjid
[\[96a.7\]]phung po bla na med/_/sangs rgyas rin chen kun 'dus pa/_/rnam par rgyal la phyag 'tshal lo/_/dbyig gi ye shes gtso mchog nyid/_/rdo rje dam pa mchog 'dzin pa'i/_/khyod ni dam tshig gtso lags kyis/_/dbang phyug rgyal pos bdag dbang bskur/_/dpa' bo chen po des gnang bas/_/oM
[\[96b\]]
[\[96b.1\]]badzra a mr-i ta a hi ha sarba maN+Dal hUM/_a be she ka hri ta/_nag po chen pos yang gsol pa/_/bdag ni skyes bu khyod kyis dbang bskur bas/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis de nyid bdag dbang bskur/_/bcom ldan thams cad mchog nyid bdag lags te/_/mchog nyid bsgrub phyir dbang rnams blang bar
[\[96b.2\]]bgyi/_/de yi rjes su 'khor rnams kyis/_/mos dang snyan pa'i tshig gsol te/_/seng ger sprul te gdan du phul/_/la las lus kyi rgyan du phul/_/la las sham thabs dag tu phul/_/la las thig ler phul byas shing /_/la las byug pas mnyes byas nas/_/la las phreng bar mdzes pa'i
[\[96b.3\]]rgyan/_/la las phyag mtshan phul te gnas/_/de nas ging gi rgyal po la/_/mnga' gsol mchod pa'i tshul du bstabs/_/nye bar spyod pa lnga yang bzhin/_/dam tshig dam rdzas bsngo ba ni/_/dka' thub chen po tshur gson cig_/legs ldan nag po ma rungs pa/_/rang gi rgyal srid la gnas te/_
[\[96b.4\]]khram la btab pa'i dgra bgegs rnams/_/rol cig dgongs shig dam tshig gtso/_/khyed kyi dam tshig dus la bab/_/bse byang khram la btab pa yi/_/ma dang sring mo bud med la/_/dpa' bo khyod kyis rol mdzod cig_/dam tshig chen pos ma btang shig_/zhe sdang can gyi bdag po rnams/_/
[\[96b.5\]]sems can kun gyi srog 'phrog pa/_/bse byang khram la btab pa yis/_/sha dang khrag la longs spyod gyis/_/gnod sbyin chen po ma rungs rnams/_/bse byang khram la btab pa yi/_/gser sogs yul 'khor blangs nas ni/_/rang gi 'dod pas longs spyod gyis/_/rtog pa'i rgyal po rnams
[\[96b.6\]]gson cig_/bse byang khram la btab pa yi/_/mgo thod bcad nas rtag rten dang /_/dge mtshan rnal 'byor ngas 'dod na/_/yid bzhin lta bu'i dngos grub gsol/_/rigs ngan sme sha can gyi tshogs/_/ba glang khyi sha rta sha dang /_/mi sha glang chen sha sogs bzhes/_/srin mo khrag 'phrog ma
[\[96b.7\]]lus la/_/bsad pa'i khrag ni dron mo dag_/bzhes shig dgra bo'i khrag la rol/_/sprul pa'i phra men chen mo rnams/_/thod rus rkang dang 'bru mar khrag_/chad dang a mr-i tar sbyar yang /_/rdzu 'phrul sgrub pa'i dam rdzas bzhes/_/rigs ngan chen po ma rungs pa/_/sha chen bshang gci khu ba
[\[97a\]]
[\[97a.1\]]khrag//dam rdzas 'bar ba 'di bzhes la/_/bdag gi nad rnams bzlog tu gsol/_/dmigs bya 'di la rims nad thong /_/srid pa'i bud med ma rungs khyed/_/bro gar glu tshig mchod bzhes/_/dmigs bya 'jo tshul stabs kyis phrogs/_/shor ba gzhon nu bdud mo'i
[\[97a.2\]]rigs/_/rnal 'byor chen po'i bka' byung gis/_/sngags sgra rang gi mchod pa bzhes/_/dmigs bya'i phung po rdul du rlog_/log 'dren can gyi gdon rnams nyon/_/yang dag nang du kun rig na/_/che chung las ni gang byas kyang /_/gnyis kyi dbang du mi 'gyur gyi/_/rnal 'byor nga yi las 'di
[\[97a.3\]]sgrubs/_/gsang tshig bsten pa'i tshogs rnams nyon/_/bshang gci khrag dang sol khu'i gos/_/brgya'am stong du gon nas ni/_/ling ka bcad na sangs rgyas 'jigs/_/dam rdzas mchod pa 'di bzhes la/_/bcol pa'i las rnams grub par gyis/_/mnga' bdag chen po ma rungs pa/_/rdo rje
[\[97a.4\]]sems dpa'i sprul pa ste/_/khro bo'i rgyal po ging chen po/_/mnga' bdag bdud kyi rgyal po bzhengs/_/rnal 'byor chen po ngas bstod cing /_/khyod kyi mthun pa'i rdzas phul bas/_/sngon gyi bskal pa bzang po la/_/khas blangs dam bcas mna' bor ba'i/_/sngon du rig 'dzin gong mas bsgrubs/_/
[\[97a.5\]]da lta rnal 'byor bdag sgrub na/_/bam ri thod pa mkhar gyi rtser/_/ru mtshon nag po pu ru ru/_/mtshon cha nag po char du phab/_/bdud bya nag po lding zhing 'jums/_/dur khrod mang po'i rgyan rnams rdzogs/_/mche gtsigs rngam pa'i zhal gdangs nas/_/khro bo khro mo'i sprul pa 'khrigs/_/
[\[97a.6\]]srin po srin mo rkan sgra rdeb/_/gnod sbyin pho mo 'brug ltar sgrogs/_/za byed pho mo glog ltar 'gyu/_/so so mos pa tha dad pa'i/_/yid bzhin nor bu dam tshig ni/_/yongs su rdzogs pas blang bar byos/_/de ltar mchod bstod byas rjes la/_/rang rgyud dam tshig gis gnas te/_/de dag rnams
[\[97a.7\]]la mthun rdzas bsngo/_/de nas ging chen 'khor bcas kyis/_/'bangs su mchi'o bdag lus 'bul/_/'bangs la nan tan ma chung cig_/de nas slan chad bka' bzhin du/_/bka' lung bzhin du rjes su bsgrub/_/gal te bka' bzhin ma bgyis na/_/dam pa'i lung las 'gal 'gyur
[\[97b\]]
[\[97b.1\]]bas/_/bdag cag rnams kyi mgo lus snying /_/rul myags skams nas tshig par 'gyur/_/ma sring bu mo chung ma rnams/_/'bangs su dbul lo rtsis ma chung /_/dbus su mchis skal mi ldan gyi/_/'bar ba'i dkyil 'khor mtha' la zhog_/phud la 'tshal skal mi ldan gyi/_/lhag ma
[\[97b.2\]]zhal chab blon la gsol/_/nye gnas gdung mo ma sring rnams/_/deng nas rgyal ba'i 'bangs yin gyi/_/khyed kyi ci bgyi las mkhan te/_/bka' yi las byung rtag par myur du bsgrub/_/ru lu ru lu b+h+yo zhes pas/_/rang gi srog la tshad du bzhag_/dpa' bo chen pos bka' stsal pa/_/brtse bar
[\[97b.3\]]byed na mar bya'o/_/gdung bar byed na sring mo ste/_/brtson par byed na bran du bya/_/byang chub dag ni bur bya'o/_/bdud bral med na slob mar bya'o/_/bskul ba mgyogs na pho nya bya'o/_/bka' bzhin byed na bka' la gdags/_/rdo rje ljags kyi 'od zer las/_/rag+sha shrI he ru ka_/ru trA ma tra ha haM zhes
[\[97b.4\]]bsdus te bzlas pa bya/_bsnyen pa bzlas pa 'bum byas la/_/don chen stsal ba zhes su bshad/_/thun mtshams kun du mchod pa yang /_/bdud chen la sogs gtang bar bya/_/don chen rnyed par gyur nas ni/_/sna yi bu ga'i hUM ring las/_/khro bo ging gi rgyal po ste/_/las kyi rgyal po srog bdag
[\[97b.5\]]ni/_/ljang sngon drag po gsal shing can/_/spros dang gnyis su med par bstim/_/rgyu zhags khar nag skud pa'am/_/mthing nag dar chen 'bar ba la/_/phye ma'i ri lu gsum sbrus te/_/rang gi lag pa g.yon par gzung /_/gzungs thag blangs te sngags bzlas pa/_/nye ba'i bsnyen pa 'bum du
[\[97b.6\]]bzlas/_/don chen bsnyen par gyur pa yi/_/de nas don la 'jug par bya/_/rang gi lag pa g.yon pa yis/_/thum po bar pa kha phye nas/_/mkhar gyi nang du pho nya bskul/_/'bum du sgrub pa dag ni bzlas/_/de nas tshogs kyi mchod pa ni/_/gsum du byas te dbul byas nas/_/gdeng du gyur
[\[97b.7\]]pa'i gsang sngags mchod/_/sgrub pa chen po 'bum du bzlas/_/pho nya mngag gzhug bdag dkyil 'khor/_/'brub khung las kyi dkyil 'khor ni/_/stug po bkod pa'i zhing khams na/_/rnam dag lam gshegs rgyal ba rnams/_/rkong rkang thang mar rgya mtsho de/_/'brub khung drag shul can
[\[98a\]]
[\[98a.1\]]gyi gnas/_/rdo rje thabs kyis blta ba'i yul/_/dur khrod bdag po tshogs dang bcas/_/bdag ni bka' yi las mkhan te/_/bka' yi las kyi dus byung bas/_/sangs rgyas kun gyis gdul dka' ba/_/de dag ma lus bdag gis gdul/_/bka' las de dag mdor
[\[98a.2\]]bkod pa'o/_/lho phyogs las kyi maN+Dal sum brtsegs la/_/dang po thod pa'i phreng bas brgyan/_/de 'og mtshon cha'i char gyis spras/_/de 'og me ri 'bar bas spras/_/nang du rgya sol nag pos byugs/_/de yi nang du ling+ga ni/_/ji lta ba yi tshul gyis gzhag_/yan lag phyag rgya bzhi yis
[\[98a.3\]]brgyangs/_/kha ran dang por phra men ma/_/bar ma la ni mgo brnyan te/_/tha ma la ni srin mo'i tshogs/_/gdug pa'i tsher ma'i phur bu la/_/mtshon par byas te rnam par bkod/_/mgul nas gdags shing rten la 'dud/_/der ni las la sbyar ba yi/_/gtor ma la sogs mchod pa rnams/_/mnyes
[\[98a.4\]]shing mgu ba gzhung bzhin bya/_/ji srid mtshan ma rnyed kyi bar/_/las la sbyor ba drug pa'i sngags/_/rngam pa'i nga ros gdon par bya/_/mnyes la sogs pa gzu dpang gsol/_/de nas pho nya mngag par bya/_/'bar ba drag po mi bzad pa'i/_/rtog pa med pa'i rgyal po las/_/rdo rje ljags kyi
[\[98a.5\]]'od zer gyis/_/badzra kro ta sa ma ya/_/khro bo rgyal po sprin phung po/_/mngag gzhug pho nyar spro bar bya/_/rag+sha dz+wa la sa ma ya/_sngon po mngag pa'i drag sngags so/_/gnod sbyin rbad pa'i drag sngags so/_/tsit+ta dz+wa la sa ma ya/_/za byed bskul ba'i pho nya'o/_/sngags dang ming du spel nas ni/_/khros
[\[98a.6\]]pas khrir ma 'bum du bzlas/_/dud chen btang la bskul ba ni/_/sngon tshe dpal chen nyid kyi bka'/_/de nas rnal 'byor rigs rgyud bka'/_/da lta rnal 'byor bdag sgrub kyis/_/khas blangs dam bcas brjed dam ci/_/dam bcas bzhin du phrin las mdzod/_/ji ltar ma byams bu la gdung ba
[\[98a.7\]]bzhin/_/dam tshig can la dung dung gdung bar gyis/_/gang du sring byams ming la gdung ba bzhin/_/dam tshig can la ltang ltang brtse bar gyis/_/mdza' bo grogs la ji ltar gdung tshul bzhin/_/rnal 'byor can la kril kril brtse bar gyis/_/ji ltar g.yog byams dpon la snying brtse
[\[98b\]]
[\[98b.1\]]bzhin/_/dam pa rnams la mnyes par nye bar gyis/_/rgyal ba kun gyi chos sku pad+ma'i gdung /_/chos rje 'od dpag med pa rdo rje chos/_/spyan ras gzigs sprul hrIHlas rngam tshul ston/_/ngag gi dbang phyug rta gdong zhabs kyis gnon/_/'jigs byed chen po 'bar ba la/_/sngo nag 'bar ba'i ral pa
[\[98b.2\]]can/_/dbu dgu phyag ni bco brgyad pa/_/rdo rje gshog pas bar snang khebs/_/ba spu lcags kyu bsregs 'dra yis/_/sdom dang sdig dang rmigs pa sbrul/_/'jigs pa'i gzugs kyis sa gzhi khebs/_/thod skyogs sti ra rgyu zhags dang /_/nyi zla khyung dang 'ug pa khra/_/rdo rje mdung rtse gsum pa dang /_
[\[98b.3\]]za ma tog dang rngul yab rnga/_/ri rab phyi skor stong gsum 'phen/_/klu dbang 'bum gyi rgyan gyis bklubs/_/dus mtha' bskal pa'i me ltar 'bar/_/khro gnyer sdang mig 'bar ba ni/_/nyi shu rtsa bdun spyan ras gzigs/_/zhabs kyis 'bar ba'i lha brgyad gnon/_/rdo rje srin po khro bor gyur/_/lha
[\[98b.4\]]dang bdun las rnam par grags/_/che mchog thugs kyi sprul pa las/_/lha chen nag po mi bzad pa/_/mtsho ni rkong rkang thang dmar na/_/ri bo byan lag mchongs kyi rtse/_/ma la ya yi rtse la lhags/_/sku gsung thugs kyi rdo rje las/_/sprul pa'i sras mchog rdo rje 'dzin/_/gzhon nu bye ba sa yar

[\[120a.3\]]ro pe a na laM be/_ta ra laM ba/_ya sho ba ti/_ma hA te dze ni ra ku le nirba Ne sarba bud+d+ha a d+hiSh+ShA na/_a d+hiSh+tha te swA hA/_gzungs 'dis sa'i gong bu'am bye ma'i gong bu la lan nyi shu rtsa gcig bzlas te mchod rten bya'o/_/de la rdul phra rab ji snyed yod pa de snyed kyi mchod rten bye ba rnams byas par
[\[120a.4\]]'gyur ro/_/rdul phra rab rnams kyi grangs dang mnyam pa'i bsod nams 'thob par 'gyur ro/_/sa'i dbang phyug tu yang 'gyur ro/_/myur du bla na med pa yang dag par rdzogs pa'i byang chub tu mngon par rdzogs par 'tshang rgya bar 'gyur ro/_/de skad du bcom ldan 'das de bzhin gshegs
[\[120a.5\]]pa rnam par snang mdzad 'od kyi rgyal pos gsungs te/_phan yon chen po dang ldan pa'i gzungs so/_/ye d+harmA he tu pra b+ha bA he tun+te ShAn+ta thA ga to h+ya ba data/_te ShA stsa yo ni rod+ha e baM bA dI ma hA shra ma NaH/_zhes bya ba'i tshigs su bcad pas rab tu gnas pa byas nas/_oM na mo b+ha ga ba te puSh+pa ke tu rA
[\[120a.6\]]dzA ya/_ta thA ga tA ya/_ar+ha te samya k+saM pud+d+hA ya/_tad+ya thA/_oM puSh+pe puSh+pe ma hA puSh+pe puSh+pe/_su puSh+po da b+ha be puSh+pa saM b+ha be puSh+pa a ba ki r+N-i swA hA/_/zhes pa'i gzungs 'dis lan bdun bsngags pa'i me tog dbul lo/_/me tog snyed de bye ba snyed kyi me tog phul bar 'gyur ro zhes so/_/
[\[120a.7\]]de nas oM na mo b+ha ga ba te rat+na ke tu rA dzA ya/_ta thA ga tA ya/_ar+ha te samya kaMs bud+d+hA ya/_tad+ya thA/_oM rat+ne rat+ne ma hA rat+ne rat+na bi dza ye swA hA/_zhes bya ba 'dis mchod rten la phyag bya'o/_/mchod rten gcig la phyag byas pas mchod rten bye ba la phyag byas par 'gyur ro/_/mchod rten
[\[120b\]]
[\[120b.1\]]la phyag bya ba'i cho ga'o/_/de nas na maHsa man+ha bud+d+ha nAM/_oM badzra A yu She swA hA/_zhes pa 'jim pa blang ba'i sngags so/_/oM badzrod b+ha bA ya swA hA/_zhes pa 'bi 'bi bya ba'i sngags so/_/oM a ra dze bi ra dze swA hA/_zhes pa 'bru mar byug pa'i sngags so/_/oM d+harma d+hA tu gar+b+he swA hA/_zhes
[\[120b.2\]]skol phor du gzhug pa'i sngags so/_/oM badzra mung+ka ra A ko Ta ya hUM phaT swA hA/_zhes pa brdung ba'i sngags so/_/oM d+harmA ba te swA hA/_skol phor nas dbyung ba'i sngags so/_/oM su pra tiSh+Tha badzre swA hA/_zhes pa bzhugs su gsol ba'i sngags so/_/oM sarba ta thA ga ta ma Ni shata dI pa te
[\[120b.3\]]dz+wA la dz+wA la d+harma d+hA tu gar+b+he swA hA/_zhes pa rab tu gnas pa'i sngags so/_/oM swa b+hA ba bi shud+d+he A ha ra A gats+tsha A gats+tsha d+harma d+hA tu gar+b+he swA hA/_zhes pa gshegs su gsol ba'i sngags so/_/oM A kA sha d+hA tu gar+b+he swA hA/_zhes pa bzod par gsol ba'i sngags so/_/'di ni sAts+tsha

[\[120b.5\]]'phags ma shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin ma la phyag 'tshal lo/_/tad+ya thA/_oM mu ni d+harme saM gra ha d+harme bi muk+ti d+ha rmes dA a mu gra ha d+ha rme bai shra ba Na pa ri brti ta d+harme sarba kA ra ya pa ri pra paN d+harme/_sa ma tA pa ri brti ta d+harme swA hA/_oM pradz+nyA shru ti smra ti bi dza ya d+hI d+hA ra Ni ye swA hA/_'di bzung
[\[120b.6\]]pas shes rab kyi pha rol tu phyin pa stong phrag brgya pa gzung bar 'gyur ro/_/na maHsa man+ta bud+d+ha nAM a pra ti ha ta shA sa nA nAM/_oM d+hu na hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA/_'di bzung bas 'phags pa ting nge 'dzin gyi rgyal po'i mdo gzung bar 'gyur ro/_/na maHsa man+ta bud+d+hA nAM a pra ti ha ta shA sa nA nAM/_oM
[\[120b.7\]]ma Ni d+ha ri badzri Ni ma hA pra ti sa re hUM hUM phaT phaT swA hA/_'di bzung bas so sor 'brang ma chen mo gzung bar 'gyur ro/_/gzungs 'di dag dang tshigs su bcad pa la sogs pa bklags te phyag byas te de nas mchod rten la sogs pa mi 'jig pa'i sa phyogs su bzhugs par bya'o/_/'di'i

[\[121a.1\]]phan yon yang bcom ldan 'das kyis mchod rten nam gzugs brnyan rnams la rdul phra rab ji snyed yod pa de snyed du nges par sa steng dang lha'i rgyal po byed par 'gyur ro/_/gzugs dang gzugs med pa'i ting nge 'dzin phun sum tshogs pa mtha' dag dang bde ba thams

[\[121a.3\]]steng dgra yi tshogs las rgyal bar 'gyur/_/zhes so/_/de'i rjes su lag par bsgoms pa'i zla ba'i dkyil 'khor gyi gdan la bzhugs pa'i b+h+rUM la sogs pa'i sa bon lnga las byung ba'i rtag pa la sogs pa zhu ba dang lhan cig 'dres pa'i chu mdun du dzaM las byung ba'i dzam+b+ha la ser po dung dang
[\[121a.4\]]pad+ma'i khar gter gyi ming can gyi gter bdag zhabs gnyis kyis mnan te bzhugs pa rdo rje nyi ma'i cod pan dang ut+pa la'i phreng ba can phyag gnyis na ne'u le dang bI dza pU ra bsnams pa bsams te/_oM dzam+b+ha la dza len+d+rA ya swA hA/_zhes pas brgya rtsa brgyad de'i spyi bor mdzub mo brkyang pas
[\[121a.5\]]sbyin par bya'o/_/dzam+b+ha la la tshu sbyin pa'i cho ga'o/_/oM dza la mi daM sarba pre te b+h+yaHswA hA/_zhes pas yi dgas thams cad la byams pas dmigs te chu sbyin no/_/de nas na maHsu rU pA ya ta thA ga tA ya/_ar+ha te samya k+saM bud+d+ha ya/_tad+ya thA/_oM su rU su rU/_pra su rU pra su rU/_ta ra ta ra/_
[\[121a.6\]]b+ha ra b+ha ra/_saM b+ha ra saM b+ha ra/_sma ra sma ra/_san+tar pa ya san+tar pa ya/_sarba pre ta nAM swA hA/_gzungs 'dis chu dang bcas pa'i zas la lan bdun yongs su bzlas te lag pa g.yon pas se gol gyi sgra lan gsum du byas nas yi dgas thams cad la dben pa'i sa phyogs su sbyin par
[\[121a.7\]]bya zhing 'di skad kyang brjod par bya ste/_skabs tshol ba dang glags lta ba rnams dengs shig_/'jig rten gyi khams thams cad na gnas pa'i yi dgas rnams la bza' ba bdag gis sbyin par bgyi'o zhes bya ba'o/_/zas ma zos pa'i sngon rol nyid du sbyin par bya'o/_/de ltar na
[\[121b\]]
[\[121b.1\]]yi dgas thams cad la 'bras bre bo che re'i bza' ba so sor byin par 'gyur ro/_/de ltar byas na skye ba nas skye bar yang nyam chung bar mi 'gyur ro/_/dbul por mi 'gyur ro/_/stobs che ba dang mdzes pa dang mthong na dga' ba dang /_phyug cing longs spyod che bar 'gyur ro/_/tshe ring zhing

[\[121b.3\]]b+ha ra saM b+ha ra hUM phaT swA hA/_sngags 'di lan bdun brjod cing lag pa g.yas pa brkyang ba'i sor mo lnga po las rnam par byung ba'i bdud rtsi lnga'i rgyun gyis sgo'i rtsar gzhag pa'i chu dang bcas pa'i gtor ma'i bza' ba mngon par gang bas 'bru nyag ma re la yul ma ga d+ha'i bre bo che khal lnga tsam

[\[121b.5\]]snyan te gling bzhi'i rnam par dag pa zla kham dang /_gru gsum dang /_zlum po dang /_gru bzhi dang /_gzhan yang mngon par 'dod pa'i maN+Dal gyi cho ga bzhin sangs rgyas la sogs pa rab tu mchod par bya'o/_/de la 'di ni cho ga ste/_rkang pa bkru ba byas nas/_oM AHbadzra snA ni hUM zhes
[\[121b.6\]]pas khrus bya ste/_oM hrIHswA hA/_zhes pas lag pa bkru ba dang kha bshal ba byas nas/_oM AHhUM zhes pa'i sngags kyis gnas dang bdag dang rnal 'byor srung ba'i cho ga bya ste/_oM hUM zhes pas stan byin gyis brlabs nas/_oM AHbadzra b+hU mi hUM zhes pas sa gzung bar bya ste/_oM

[\[123a.1\]]chub sems dpa' rnams kyi mdun du mchod pa'i sprin rnams ji ltar bsams pa bzhin bden par gnas par 'gyur ro/_/sku khrus kyi mchod pa yang /_oM AHsarba ta thA ga ta a b+hi She ka ta sa ma ya shri ye hUM swA hA/_zhes pas sku khrus byas la sngar bzhin mchod pa la sogs

[\[123b\]]
[\[123b.1\]]par bya'o/_/na maHsarba bud+d+ha bo d+hi sa twA nAM sarba tra saM ku su mi ta a b+hi dz+nyA rA si ni na mo stu te swA hA/_zhes pa'o/_/bdag skye ba nas skye bar sangs rgyas la gus pa dang /_rang bzhin gyis g.yo med pa dang /_sems can thams cad la byams pa dang /_gtong ba la goms pa dang /_'bras

[\[124a.1\]]'bebs shing /_/lo tog phun sum tshogs par shog_/rgyal po chos bzhin byed gyur cig_/'jig rten dag kyang dar bar shog_/ngan song sdug bsngal ma myong zhing /_/dka' ba spyad pa med par yang /_/lha bas lhag pa'i lus kyis ni/_/de dag sangs rgyas myur grub

[\[207a.1\]]dang /_bsam pa'i yul gnyis la cher sems shing de nyid la dpa' ba'i phyir ro/_/nyan thos dang zhes bya ba ni/_sgo bzhir zhugs nas rgyu 'bras brgyad po sgrub cing thob pa'i skyes bu dag go/_/ci'i phyir zhe na/_rdzu 'phrul gyi rna ba lta bus zhal nas gsungs pa dag thos
